# Welcome | Adaptix Framework

AdaptixC2 is ​​an extensible post-exploitation and adversarial emulation framework made for penetration testers. The Adaptix Server is written in Golang and to allow operator flexibility. The GUI Client is written in C++ QT, allowing it to be used on Linux, Windows, and MacOS operating systems.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FYEOzDBDWeUK6Nme5lgoR%252FScreenshot_20260114_212634.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da3864c4f-107c-4454-b07a-9a60ca026de9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dd78580d&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework#features)

Features


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Server/Client Architecture for Multiplayer Support
    
*   Cross-platform GUI client
    
*   Fully encrypted communications
    
*   Listener and Agents as Plugin (Extender)
    
*   Task and Jobs storage
    
*   Files and Process browsers
    
*   Credentials, Targets and Screenshots Managers
    
*   Socks4 / Socks5 / Socks5 Auth support
    
*   Local and Reverse port forwarding support
    
*   BOF support
    
*   Linking Agents and Sessions Graph
    
*   Agents Health Checker
    
*   Agents KillDate and WorkingTime control
    
*   Windows/Linux/MacOs agents support
    
*   Remote Terminal / Shell
    
*   AxScript Engine
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework#agents)

Current Extenders


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   HTTP/S Beacon Listener
    
*   SMB Beacon Listener
    
*   TCP Beacon Listener
    
*   DNS/DoH Beacon Listener
    
*   Beacon Agent
    
*   TCP/mTLS Gopher Listener
    
*   Gopher Agent
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework#agents-1)

Extension-Kit


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 on GitHub

# v0.1 -> v0.2 | Adaptix Framework

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FmNVXcQ5NX8BGBiBIK5MO%252F0.2%2520Update.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D679ca34d-dde7-47c0-a636-142395e929f5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed0bcd0&sv=2)

**AdaptixC2**

*   AdaptixC2 adds interface support for working with Socks4 and Socks5 proxy server versions (with support for authentication, TCP/UDP, IPv4 and DNS, but not IPv6). [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/tunnels-and-forwarding)
    
*   AdaptixC2 adds interface support for working with Local and Reverse TCP port forwarding. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/tunnels-and-forwarding)
    
*   AdaptixC2 improves server-client interaction;
    
*   AdaptixC2 extenders are specified in the server profile, not through a separate file. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting#adaptixserver)
    
*   The AdaptixServer profile now has the ability to customize the server's response to illegitimate request. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting#adaptixserver)
    
*   Computer field added to TasksTable in AdaptixClient;
    
*   User field added to DownloadsTable in AdaptixClient;
    
*   Changed the Logs panel of AdaptixClient;
    
*   Added the ability to connect one client to multiple servers. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#id-1.-projects)
    
*   Light theme added to AdaptixClient;
    
*   In AdaptixClient after agent generation a window with the path to the saved file has been added;
    
*   The listener creation and agent generation dialogs now have the option to save the current configuration to a file and load it from a file;
    
*   In AdaptixClient, the Ctrl+A (Select All) keyboard shortcut now works in all tables;
    
*   In AdaptixClient, the Ctrl+L (Clear Console) keyboard shortcut now works in the agent console;
    
*   In AdaptixClient, when navigating through the command history, the command entered before navigating through the history is now cached;
    
*   AdaptixClient now has the ability to customize the interface. You can select a theme and font settings, customize the time display format in the agent console, and select fields that will not be displayed in the SessionsTable;
    
*   In AdaptixClient, the Commander class responsible for parsing arguments has been fixed;
    
*   A guide on how to create a Windows client has been added to the documentation. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-server#windows-1)
    

**Agent Beacon:**

*   The Beacon agent supports Socks4 and Socks5 proxy servers (with support for authentication, TCP/UDP, IPv4 and DNS, but not IPv6);
    
*   The Beacon agent support for working with Local and Reverse TCP port forwarding;
    
*   Added BOF API: BeaconUseToken, BeaconRevertToken;
    
*   AgentExteneder now validates data received from the agent;
    
*   Fixed agent termination function. Agent correctly informs about termination;
    
*   Fixed a bug in the agent: if the server was unavailable, the agent cached the server as unavailable and did not contact it anymore.
    

**Extension-Kit:**

*   Add [Kerbeus-BOFarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/Extension-Kit/tree/main/Kerbeus-BOF)
    
*   Add [Aliasesarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/Extension-Kit/tree/main/Aliases)
    

Last updated 1 year ago

---

# v0.4 -> v0.5 | Adaptix Framework

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.4-greater-than-v0.5#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   AdaptixClient now features a **RemoteTerminal** — a fully interactive console
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FLM5q0IM8mPs1iaXRFVNC%252FScreenshot_20250528_181244.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2c6b673c-8482-464b-bd47-744f2ae30218&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71a65365&sv=2)

*   Tunnels can now be created from the **context menu** of the session table or the graph. It is now possible to build tunnels via AdaptixClient (**clienside**), not just through Teamserver. The tunnel mechanism has been reworked to correctly handle SSL frame formation. Information about whether a specific type of tunnel is supported by the agent is included in the tunnel configuration
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F00sBqyr0gR0UcSEtm4nG%252FScreenshot_20250528_133227.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1632792c-fa25-4769-8a92-6cb0d11123d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=38eb333a&sv=2)

*   Command parameters can now have an empty default value
    
*   Screenshot zoom is now limited to values between x0.3 and x4.0
    
*   Columns in the TasksTable have been updated. Active tunnels are now marked as **Running** instead of **Hosted**
    
*   A [**Blogs**](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/blogs)
     section with public materials about AdaptixC2 has been added to the documentation.
    

**Fix:**

*   New methods are now used for newer versions of Qt libraries instead of deprecated ones
    
*   Indentation in tables no longer relies on QtDelegate — it is now fully implemented using QSS styles. This resolves the issue of colored spaces appearing in some tables
    
*   Fixed an issue where the client window could shrink on startup
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.4-greater-than-v0.5#agent-beacon)

Agent Beacon


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Add Custom BOF API `AxAddScreenshot`
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed the header value processing mechanism in the **BeaconHTTP** listener: [Pull Request #53arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/AdaptixC2/pull/53)
     (by [D4rthMaulCoparrow-up-right](https://github.com/D4rthMaulCop)
    )
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.4-greater-than-v0.5#agent-gopher)

Agent Gopher


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Added Windows support
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FIpv0YM6m7prdaTjxcEG0%252FScreenshot_20250528_181011.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80727a31-87c1-4553-b83d-5bd2a4fe868f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f44e8330&sv=2)

*   Support for multithreaded parallel SOCKS5 tunnels has been implemented.
    
*   Added **Cancel** function to the Downloads Storage
    
*   Added **Exit** option to the context menu in the session table and the graph
    
*   **FilesBrowser** now supports both file **download** and **upload**
    

**Fix:**

*   Symbolic links are now recognized, and **FilesBrowser** correctly displays them as either files or directories
    
*   File downloads were previously very slow due to a chunk size of only 10 bytes. The default chunk size for downloads is now 1 MB
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.4-greater-than-v0.5#extension-kit)

Extension-Kit


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New BOFs:**

*   Postex-BOF: `screenshot_bof`

# v0.3 -> v0.4 | Adaptix Framework

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.3-greater-than-v0.4#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Added control over **WorkingTime** and **KillDate** parameters for agents. Added new agent marks "**Disconnect**" and "**No worktime**".
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FM8r3q0I9enlktuGSnD2F%252FScreenshot_20250427_223011.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De17455c7-334a-423c-9dba-29643ce8cf44&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e1e6a52&sv=2)

*   Added screenshot storage.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FL4ZZEFOnOkESNxeE7FdZ%252FScreenshot_20250427_214233.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59350efe-0a44-462e-b6b3-f8b65e89691c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f3b161bf&sv=2)

*   Unix support added to **ProcessBrowser** and **FilesBrowser**.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F7n72Cnx4q2lpewi9AOML%252FScreenshot_20250427_123146.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dafa804fb-abd9-436a-9e5d-7251019570de&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=366fddfd&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FrdGg0MYM1wfPQE3EDSMg%252FScreenshot_20250427_123332.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D15c82b18-79f6-4c88-8c17-00054d8ee7d6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bdd4a6d6&sv=2)

*   **SessionsGraph** now displays the agent type and process PID instead of the process name.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FBefZEtp0IGKTaFlWtSO9%252FScreenshot_20250427_230905.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97f98e40-c038-499c-b706-7cee4a229206&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3beb5b7&sv=2)

*   New form of agent generation. The mechanisms for registering listeners and agents have been completely changed.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FFrwpaSbFIu7gv8PoyLei%252FScreenshot_20250427_130106.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D40d62ea5-52f4-4d72-800a-62ca8457e1be&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5e9076a3&sv=2)

*   The listeners table has been reworked.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FdQwWexgecuhfOuQctjGR%252FScreenshot_20250427_122049.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e56bc0d-93aa-4626-8e6e-876ed81a2094&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a89e0226&sv=2)

*   Added "**vspacer**", "**hspacer**", "**time\_input**", "**date\_input**" elements to WidgetBuilder. More details
    
*   For extensions, the functions `$RAND(len, charmap)`, `$HASH(algorithm, len, data)`, `$MAP(map, key)` are implemented. [More details](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#id-1.-command)
    
*   Completely new mechanism for connecting extenders. Now all information about the extender is contained in a single JSON configuration file. All common structures are now loaded from the [axc2arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/axc2)
     package. Server operation has become much faster. More variability in developing agents for different listeners and operating systems.
    
*   Added formatting to the downloads, processes and files tables.
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed message in agent console. Previously there were extra characters `.` when there was no domain.
    
*   Fixed display of sleep time
    
*   Fixed incorrect escaping of quotes when entering an agent console command.

NEW GOPHER AGENT


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Added a new synchronous gopher agent that supports Linux and MacOS systems.
    
*   A TCP/mTLS listener has been added to the agent.
    
*   This agent currently has limited functionality.

Agent Beacon

*   Added TCP internal communication channel
    
*   Added **WorkingTime** and **KillDate** functions
    
*   The listener creation form and agent profile have been changed. Now each Callback Server has its own port.
    
*   Added BOF API: `BeaconAddValue`, `BeaconGetValue`, `BeaconRemoveValue`.
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed the function of determining the file modification date.
    
*   The DLL agent supports launching via rundll32 (by [melnicekarrow-up-right](https://github.com/melnicek)
    ).

# Getting Starting | Adaptix Framework

The Adaptix server is installed only on UNIX systems.

The following operating systems have been tested for Adaptix Client compatibility:

*   Ubuntu 25.04
    
*   Debian 11
    
*   Arch 2025.02.01
    
*   Kali Linux 2024.4
    
*   Windows 10 / 11
    
*   MacOS Sonoma
    

[Installation Serverchevron-right](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-server)
[Startingchevron-right](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting)

Last updated 1 month ago

# v0.6 -> v0.7 | Adaptix Framework

circle-exclamation

Extension-Kit extensions need to be reinstalled

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.6-greater-than-v0.7#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   **Added Credential Manager**
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FID2mES4X6UgMzL9ONbkS%252FScreenshot_20250728_181635.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61057243-e551-4475-b1b4-8aa734803ca3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a75449a4&sv=2)

*   Implemented the **AxScript scripting engine**. Added **AxScript Console** for testing AX scripts and displaying error information from user scripts.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FzMyDGyMYJNLQR6HXnY7N%252FScreenshot_20250728_185414.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D17a21b0b-55b8-4391-92dd-87f1d3f76cba&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b5769b70&sv=2)

*   The **menu in the Sessions table and Sessions graph** is now generated using AxScript. The **FileBrowser menu** is now generated using AxScript. The **DownloadsManager menu** is now generated using AxScript.
    
*   Registration of **'listener'** and **'agent'** extenders is now done through AxScript. The extender model has been significantly simplified.
    
*   It is now possible to set the **127.0.0.1** address for the Teamserver.
    
*   Help output in the client is now formatted.
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed multithreading issues when working with tunnels.
    
*   Dockerfile updated to the required Go version.
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.6-greater-than-v0.7#agent-beacon)

Agent Beacon


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Added detection of **Windows Server 2025** (by [Xre0uSarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    ).
    
*   Added additional validation for data received from the server (by [Xre0uSarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    ).
    
*   Implemented Beacon DLL execution via **rundll32** (by [**0xShkk**arrow-up-right](https://github.com/0xShkk)
    ).
    
*   Rewritten the **BOF loader** implementation.
    
*   The agent no longer determines the **impersonation token**.
    
*   Added **Execute** and **Remove** menu items in FileBrowser.
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed a potential agent hang during connection failure (by [Xre0uSarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    ).
    
*   Listener: fixed **X-Forwarded-For** header check function (by [Xre0uSarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    ).
    
*   Fixed **BeaconFormatAlloc** function, which could cause Beacon to crash (by [_undefo_arrow-up-right](https://github.com/undefo)
    ).
    
*   The `ps run` command now correctly passes arguments to the application.
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.6-greater-than-v0.7#agent-gopher)

Agent Gopher


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Added **BOF support** for Windows (by [_undefo_arrow-up-right](https://github.com/undefo)
    ).
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F8Eq2ZvspeOivIebQZeBj%252FScreenshot_20250728_184800.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ec7e5a6-b556-43a8-8ce6-b3fe73354c43&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8d45e896&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FwC71AXf7cVh6ivqZtdkh%252FScreenshot_20250728_184927.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D147211e7-781b-40c9-8de0-c6b71f6cb86c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=940d3df7&sv=2)

*   Updated the `run` command: now requires specifying the target program directly, rather than running through `cmd.exe` or `/bin/sh`.
    
*   Added `rev2self` command.

# v1.1 -> v1.2 | Adaptix Framework

circle-info

Contributors to the GitHub update include: [Hesti4arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Hesti4)
, [Sakura529arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Sakura529)
, [LongWayHomiearrow-up-right](https://github.com/LongWayHomie)
, [BlackMeerkatarrow-up-right](https://github.com/BlackMeerkat)
, [sagiolarrow-up-right](https://github.com/sagiol)
, [shashinmaarrow-up-right](https://github.com/shashinma)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v1.1-greater-than-v1.2#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

Building the client now requires QT > 6.8.0. If your Linux system uses a different version by default, use Docker to build the AppImage file.

**New:**

*   Added static AppImage client build to Docker. Windows builds are now performed using a batch script via MSYS2.
    
*   AxScript now has a full server implementation. Scripts can be loaded via a profile file.
    
*   The server no longer stores data in memory. All data processing is performed directly in the database.
    
*   Web socket authentication is now performed only via OTP tokens.
    
*   QSS themes are no longer used, and most old fonts have been removed from the client application. To ensure a consistent appearance across all systems, screen resolutions, zoom levels, and other settings, QLementine styles have been selected. The default font is now JetBrains Mono, and for the terminal, Hack.
    
*   You can now specify a custom application style and a console style in the settings.
    
*   The ability to notify about events in Slack, Telegram, and WebHook has been removed from TeamServer.
    
*   The method for transferring files and data (more than 3 MB) from the client to the server has been updated and optimized.
    
*   New WEB API: `/screen/image`, `/agent/command/raw`.
    

**Fix:**

*   Now the listener is saved even if its start was unsuccessful.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v1.1-greater-than-v1.2#beacon)

Beacon


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Implemented Async BOF function.
    
*   The `ps run` command now supports the `-i` flag, a new process will be started with the current session token.
    
*   Multiple URIs, User-Agents, and Host Headers with rotation: the HTTP beacon now supports configuring multiple values for URIs, User-Agents, and Host Headers (by [Hesti4arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Hesti4)
    )
    
*   Rotation modes (sequential / random): a new "Rotation Mode" option in the agent build config lets operators choose between round-robin (sequential) and randomized rotation for all rotating fields (servers, URIs, UAs, Host Headers) (by [Hesti4arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Hesti4)
    )
    
*   Active round-robin for servers: server rotation now happens on every callback (not only on failure), distributing traffic across all configured C2 addresses (by [Hesti4arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Hesti4)
    )
    
*   Add IAT Hiding support (by [Hesti4arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Hesti4)
    )
    

**Fix:**

*   Fix infinite recursion issue in GetSymbolAddress when handling API Set DLLs (by [Sakura529arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Sakura529)
    )
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v1.1-greater-than-v1.2#gopher)

Gopher


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Implemented Async BOF function
    
*   Implement C-style printf specifiers and BeaconFormat API suite
    

**Fix:**

*   Prevent GC from collecting DataExtract buffers

# Listeners and Agents | Adaptix Framework

Listeners are managed through the context menu of the listener tables.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FfxjTiGQIOHmnwjHrrkgq%252FScreenshot_20250828_113711.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D10e4b9b6-a795-49bf-9739-fcc82fe9dcd1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db867217&sv=2)

*   AxScript new functions: [ids](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#ids)
    , [isactive](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#isactive)
    , [format\_size](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#format_size)

    , [targets\_add\_list](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#targets_add_list)
    , [credentials\_add\_list](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#credentials_add_list)
    , [prompt\_confirm](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#prompt_confirm)
    . Also added [get\_commands](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#get_commands)
    , [validate\_command](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#validate_command)

     (by [shantanu561993arrow-up-right](https://github.com/shantanu561993)
    )
    
*   AxScript new selector: [selector\_agents](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axselector-type#selectoragents)
    
*   AxScript new menu: [add\_targets](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axmenu-type#targets-manager-menu)
    , [add\_credentials](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axmenu-type#credentials-manager-menu)
    
*   AxScript new data models: [downloads](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#downloads)
    , [screenshots](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#screenshots)
    , [tunnels](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#tunnels)
    , [targets](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#targets)

    , [on\_disconnect](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axevent-type#on_disconnect)
    , [list](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axevent-type#on_list)
    , [remove](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axevent-type#on_remove)
    .
    
*   AxScript: added [timers](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axevent-type#on_timeout)
     and [intervals](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axevent-type#on_interval)
     (by [shantanu561993arrow-up-right](https://github.com/shantanu561993)
    )
    
*   Client: added new custom theme _Fallout3_ and font **VT323** (by [Steve0roarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Steve0ro)
    )
    
*   Credentials Manager:
    
    *   added ability to set a tag.
        
    *   added ability to add or remove a list of credentials in a single request.
        
    
*   Telegram Callback: Now supports events for adding new credentials to Credentials Manager and for file download completion from remote host.
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed unintended task termination in AxScript hook handler.
    
*   Fixed premature connection closure during Reverse Port Forwarding **(**NTLM Relay now works correctly) (by [T1ernoarrow-up-right](https://github.com/T1erno)
    )

# v0.8 -> v0.9 | Adaptix Framework

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.8-greater-than-v0.9#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Rewrote the client core — the client now uses a dock-based structure.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F1B6aWVVxDmiuEB3XrMrQ%252FScreenshot_20250927_213254.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab0f5423-8d11-4bb3-97bd-c4eff8e478c1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7ebff42c&sv=2)

*   AxScript new functions: [agent\_hide](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#agent_hide)
    , [agent\_remove](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#agent_remove)
    , [hash](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#hash)
    , [random\_string](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#random_string)
    , [random\_int](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#random_int)
    .
    
*   Added new API `POST /agent/task/save` to save a task to the Tasks Manager.
    
*   Remote Terminal: you can now select a command response and save it to the Tasks Manager.
    
*   After server sync, files downloaded in DownloadsManager are now sorted by date.
    
*   Added a multithreaded client build.
    
*   Server web-APIs [published](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/web-api)
    .
    
*   Authentication: users can now authenticate to the server either with a master password or with credentials hard-coded in the profile. (by [exil-securityarrow-up-right](https://github.com/exil-security)
    )
    
*   Optimised Exist DB functions — the Exist functions now query IDs directly instead of iterating through all rows. (by [Xre0uSarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    )
    
*   Added a confirmation dialog when deleting a listener. (by [newBBnewarrow-up-right](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    
*   In addition to Telegram notifications, added the ability to notify any web service (for example ntfy.sh, Slack, or Microsoft Teams). (by [mdube99arrow-up-right](https://github.com/mdube99)
    )
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed a bug where the client login configuration would not update. (by [newBBnewarrow-up-right](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    
*   Fixed a bug where the agent command configuration would not update when the user re-logged in. (by [newBBnewarrow-up-right](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )

# Starting | Adaptix Framework

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting#adaptixserver)

AdaptixServer


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The necessary parameters for starting the AdaptixServer can be passed via command line parameters or via a configuration file.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FFVyygaIfLH5Nxjp7Xhku%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0_20260228_212214.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52417844-8b02-424a-a6e3-c12e4a3b0763&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=732aec10&sv=2)

The configuration file is specified in the `-profile` parameter and must contain a profile in YAML format.

**Teamserver**:

*   **port** - port for client connection
    
*   **endpoint** - URN for connecting clients
    
*   **password** - authenticator for clients
    
*   **only\_password** — If `true`, only password authentication is used for any login (Cobalt Strike mode). If `false`, authentication is used with strictly defined logins and passwords.
    
*   **cert** and **key** - SSL Certificate and Key for web server
    
*   **extender** - array of strings-paths to go-plugins
    
*   **axscripts -** array of strings-paths to AX Scripts
    
*   **access\_token\_live\_hours** & **refresh\_token\_live\_hours** - The validity period of the JWT token that the client receives after authorization.
    

**ServerResponse:**

*   error.status - web server response code in case of an illegitimate request
    
*   error.headers - web server HTTP Headers
    
*   error.page - the path to the file whose contents will be returned in the web server's response
    
*   http - HTTP server settings
    
*   tls - HTTP server cipher settings
    

To run adaptixserver you need an SSL certificate. You can generate your own using the ssl\_gen script.

After starting AdaptixServer, a `data` directory will be created next to the server executable file. The server database file and all other files will be created in the `data` directory.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FYIWWiuqFtfDkrB69gGAW%252FScreenshot_20260129_110737.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D67432801-2f80-4bd3-94ad-6d90d6df783b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4c97d915&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting#adaptixclient)

AdaptixClient


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After the AdaptixClient is launched, a directory named `.adaptix` will be created in the user's home directory. The AdaptixClient database file will be saved in the `.adaptix` directory. In the authorization form, you must specify the profile data, user nickname (any nick), and the name of the local project.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F9hdgkGqMp24rMLbvgPDn%252FScreenshot_20260129_105731.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0caee325-eadd-4398-b671-a9598b91b938&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1bf6c89f&sv=2)

When authorizing, you can select which data will be synchronized with the server.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FEZNwKxARcKh73m1SLfIR%252FScreenshot_20260129_105805.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D21f1f91f-1a97-4743-8b61-1046714316d3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fcec7e0c&sv=2)

After synchronizing data with the server, the main AdaptixClient window will be available.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FOKYspOwQrc2jrNGCby4E%252FScreenshot_20251229_204430.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7a3f02d-8018-4f6d-a965-d239b52f2fd0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a25e0015&sv=2)

[PreviousInstallation Clientchevron-left](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-client)
[NextUser Interfacechevron-right](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [AdaptixServer](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting#adaptixserver)
    
*   [AdaptixClient](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/starting#adaptixclient)
    

Copy

    Teamserver:
      interface: "0.0.0.0"
      port: 4321
      endpoint: "/endpoint"
      password: "pass"
      only_password: true
      operators:
        operator1: "pass1"
        operator2: "pass2"
      cert: "server.rsa.crt"
      key: "server.rsa.key"
      extenders:
        - "extenders/beacon_listener_http/config.yaml"
        - "extenders/beacon_listener_smb/config.yaml"
        - "extenders/beacon_listener_tcp/config.yaml"
        - "extenders/beacon_listener_dns/config.yaml"
        - "extenders/beacon_agent/config.yaml"
        - "extenders/gopher_listener_tcp/config.yaml"
        - "extenders/gopher_agent/config.yaml"
      axscripts:
    #    - "Extension-Kit/extension-kit.axs"
      access_token_live_hours: 12
      refresh_token_live_hours: 168
    
    HttpServer:
      error:
        status: 404
        headers:
          Content-Type: "text/html; charset=UTF-8"
          Server: "AdaptixC2"
          Adaptix-Version: "v1.2"
        page: "404page.html"
      http:
        max_header_bytes: 8192
        read_header_timeout_sec: 0
        read_timeout_sec: 0
        write_timeout_sec: 0
        idle_timeout_sec: 0
        request_timeout_sec: 300
        request_timeout_message: "504 Gateway Timeout"
        disable_keep_alives: false
        enable_http2: true
      tls:
        min_version: "TLS1.2"
        max_version: "TLS1.3"
        prefer_server_cipher_suites: false
        cipher_suites:
          - "TLS_ECDHE_RSA_WITH_AES_128_GCM_SHA256"
          - "TLS_ECDHE_RSA_WITH_AES_256_GCM_SHA384"
          - "TLS_ECDHE_ECDSA_WITH_AES_128_GCM_SHA256"
          - "TLS_ECDHE_ECDSA_WITH_AES_256_GCM_SHA384"
          - "TLS_RSA_WITH_AES_128_GCM_SHA256"
          - "TLS_RSA_WITH_AES_256_GCM_SHA384"

Copy

    openssl req -x509 -nodes -newkey rsa:2048 -keyout server.rsa.key -out server.rsa.crt -days 3650

Copy

    ./adaptixserver -profile profile.yaml

# Process Browser | Adaptix Framework

The Process Browser displays information about processes. When the Process Browser is launched, **no requests are made to the server**. To send a request to the server, you must click the Refresh button ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FwaspTq83XEWIT06VALQu%252F40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3343f776-f79c-40a7-beea-dd4db5448f1c&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e42f943&sv=2).

The Process Browser on the left displays the processes in a tree view. The table on the right displays detailed information about the processes. The current process running the agent is displayed in red.

Windows

Unix

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FwaeMfB6yipzBwiLdpcJd%252F41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d8549cc-4cee-4892-adf3-dfd09d57be26&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a812f9c0&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F3DLZZPemqW27QULUxDdY%252FScreenshot_20250427_123332.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df02f6753-3c37-434a-8c56-a28706005dc6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d011aac3&sv=2)

The "Wait" status indicates that the request is currently being processed. The "Ok" status displays the date and time of the response.

Wait

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FNgRJ5ZJGq7rogodRhkME%252F42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5337b2cb-95ca-43f8-b176-8fdf8606585a&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d1bc11c&sv=2)

Ok

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fm4fnP0DGgBKM80XUVzBF%252F43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da552190a-0f5a-444a-8e58-5da7129e26d0&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2c1a6228&sv=2)

File Browser allows you to filter processes by a substring from any column.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FJiPsD4hcekv79NbB7ykN%252F44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D000f9dc3-8a6b-4434-ab13-7ccba6e89264&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d082616&sv=2)

From the context menu of the process table you can copy the PID of the selected process.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FZMztJ1rtAwAHqM0cGJtZ%252F45.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a9d6bba-14c7-4bbe-a264-a757077ac699&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff0e9dae&sv=2)

# File Browser | Adaptix Framework

File Browser is an opportunity to explore the files on a compromised system. The left-hand side of the file browser is a tree which organizes the known drives and folders into one view. The right-hand side of the file browser shows the contents of the current folder.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fri5Gmw65rVtvIOv5gfch%252F25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8d1ba232-0b19-4874-bce8-84220c78a31c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff569264&sv=2)

When you launch the File Browser, **no request is made to the server**. If the path is empty, you can click the "Refresh" button ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F4YdqCaD4hDCPRAqsir1J%252F26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db9d24dab-701f-4bba-850f-9de0040b9a78&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12c16499&sv=2), after which the contents of the working directory will be requested. Another option: specify the desired directory in the path field and click the "Go to" button ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F6x2zTGNu0RskJV7BhPw1%252F27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc236c80d-ca6a-4234-9127-191e004c33d2&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=21d672c9&sv=2).

Windows

Unix

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fpj2mle4HbU3ElTO4oRYw%252F28.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D206f6bb0-b495-4bbd-acf4-833c1fc75057&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b5a4be0&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FzcXxHRAypMZqKX65vUnI%252FScreenshot_20250427_123146.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D790e0d55-a0c9-4588-b92f-dc790f8f9961&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1161d7e&sv=2)

After each request, File Browser caches the contents of the requested directory. An open folder ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F9PCFB2ESjKci5yOFlqLv%252F29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcaff5d49-c772-4555-b3c8-efd4d1b1044c&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9041f2b0&sv=2) (as opposed to a closed folder ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FzJ9UMZNlqA0mAQR8gowf%252F30.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad3084e6-cfe2-4924-a6ad-4c703d47c017&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=630992db&sv=2)) indicates that the folder's contents have been cached. You can navigate to cached folders without creating a new file listing request. Click "Refresh" to refresh the contents of the current folder. Double-clicking on a directory in the table or directory tree will cause the browser to navigate to that directory. To go up a level, click the folder button ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Foylq2ykL1DPz7e9y1ACr%252F34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87daa456-a81f-4b19-a54e-ba1cf511b415&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6cc425b5&sv=2) next to the file path.

Along with the directory contents, its status is also cached. The "wait" status indicates that the request is currently being processed. The "Ok" status displays the date and time the response was cached. The "Error" status contains additional information about the cause of the error.

Wait

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FEJc1v5H5DWzP76RTCREI%252F31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D069b054e-53e5-4531-ac7f-0c58d8c871ed&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=55c71f7f&sv=2)

Ok

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FC4PuOkTAO2zaJHI9z8V9%252F32.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8507c6d7-19bb-4e97-bef9-7a44b223f4dc&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f16373e&sv=2)

Error

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FyRzwtfVHo43vRtroes8A%252F33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D76435941-6522-4cc0-b395-c412e47fe33a&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d95f5855&sv=2)

To upload a file to the current directory, you can use the "Upload" button ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fp3aahwCRl4lA0Sh8gxda%252F35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28b0f719-7003-4749-a683-6c99fec29211&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2091b3f2&sv=2). To download a file from the host, you can use the command from the context menu.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FotSTpeZrcKVb4OZewFQZ%252F36.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd70af61c-f8dd-40dd-ba66-6abdddad9560&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2cf74f69&sv=2)

To see which drives are available, press "Disks" button ![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fd0BuMBWpjOiY4hUiQ4Pc%252F37.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bc2fc29-bb96-4e01-aa46-b18688f9ac0e&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ac4e2c&sv=2).

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fu9L83ONUaD1CpFqFSnbr%252F38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da685e5c7-d4a9-488b-a197-1522ad8b7aeb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=efc2369d&sv=2)

The file browser supports working not only with local disks, but also with network shared directories.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FHTB4Tc2CB4cxFZgLqRox%252F39.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6654867f-82ce-481c-9588-f5ea9376b2fa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c58d2713&sv=2)

# Installation Server | Adaptix Framework

The [source code arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/AdaptixC2)
of AdaptixС2 is available on github. The `main` branch is a stable version and does not contain the latest changes.

Copy

    git clone https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/AdaptixC2.git
    cd AdaptixC2

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-server#preinstall)

Preinstall


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-info

Adaptix teamserver is designed to run on a Linux server. To build extenders you need updated Mingw. Advice on building server and extenders (**tested**): using Ubuntu 24, Debian 12, or Dockerfile.

To build Server and Extenders, you need to install additional dependencies. Please note that _golang 1.25.4_ is required to compile and run AdaptixServer (and special [patched golangarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/go-win7)
 for win7 gopher agent).

Auto

Manual

For Linux, you can use a specially prepared script that will install and configure the necessary packages for both the server and client parts. Link — [pre\_install\_linux\_all.sharrow-up-right](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Adaptix-Framework/AdaptixC2/refs/heads/main/pre_install_linux_all.sh)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F73hLkX7874aTss7jqiOv%252FScreenshot_20251230_174450.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4a3e60c2-bd38-497a-a8af-1c0a6de79c47&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=603a207c&sv=2)

Copy

    sudo apt install mingw-w64 make gcc g++ g++-mingw-w64
    
    wget https://go.dev/dl/go1.25.4.linux-amd64.tar.gz -O /tmp/go1.25.4.linux-amd64.tar.gz
    sudo rm -rf /usr/local/go /usr/local/bin/go
    sudo tar -C /usr/local -xzf /tmp/go1.25.4.linux-amd64.tar.gz
    sudo ln -s /usr/local/go/bin/go /usr/local/bin/go
    
    # for windows 7 support by gopher agent
    git clone https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/go-win7 /tmp/go-win7
    sudo mv /tmp/go-win7 /usr/lib/

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-server#build-on-server)

Build on Server


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

AdaptixServer and Extenders (goplugins) must be built **with the same version of the golang** package.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F0gMlauK6viAZlXKwLcR7%252FScreenshot_20251127_005035.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6c6e954-763f-4c89-a706-a273da77044f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c37725d5&sv=2)

All compiled files will be located in the dist directory.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FAMFZtrgFlrJ5dfdsrPEC%252FScreenshot_20251127_005109.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D304eaf5e-2cce-4f5d-a8d1-dbc0a879b4a8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8641d80e&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-server#build-in-docker)

Build in Docker


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The compiled files will be located in the `AdaptixServer/server-dist` directory.

Profile

Description

`make docker-build-server`

Build server only

`make docker-build-extenders`

Build extenders only

`make docker-build-ext`

Build server and extenders together

`make docker-up`

Server runtime container

Added Docker cleanup targets for better build artifact management:

*   `docker-clean`: Remove Docker containers and images (builders only)
    
    *   Removes containers and images for `build-server`, `build-extenders`, and `build-server-ext` profiles
        
    *   Preserves runtime container
        
    
*   `docker-clean-all`: Remove all Docker artifacts (containers, images, volumes, networks)
    
    *   Removes all build profiles including runtime
        
    *   Cleans build output directories (`AdaptixServer/server-dist`)
        
    *   Complete cleanup for fresh rebuilds
        
    

[PreviousGetting Startingchevron-left](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting)
[NextInstallation Clientchevron-right](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-client)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Preinstall](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-server#preinstall)
    
*   [Build on Server](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-server#build-on-server)
    
*   [Build in Docker](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-server#build-in-docker)
    

Copy

    make server-ext

# Remote Terminal / Shell | Adaptix Framework

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/agent-browsers/remote-terminal-shell#remote-terminal)

Remote Terminal


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The **Remote Terminal** allows you to launch an application or command shell in fully interactive mode. For each operating system, you can either select an appropriate shell from a predefined list or specify one manually.

Linux

Windows

MacOS

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FJCMXEJM4cjCekf3Ia88d%252FScreenshot_20250528_175638.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D00bb7aa8-b67e-474a-9397-cabfcebb461d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=59e7652d&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/agent-browsers/remote-terminal-shell#remote-shell)

Remote Shell


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Remote Shell feature allows you to run applications or command shells in pseudo shell mode. For each operating system, you can either select the appropriate shell from a predefined list or specify it manually.

Some shells, such as cmd.exe in echo mode, can duplicate input and output. To eliminate this duplication, use **smart mode**.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FtUwKjJvXemqTyUmd2Cyx%252FScreenshot_20251229_223421.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc25fc712-b5e1-44b5-bfd4-ba96c3f4eaa6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=636e14dc&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FJUYvEnZ2UvTWu7bJk727%252FScreenshot_20251229_223401.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57392be4-5675-4a2f-b318-c96ffe94a362&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=43ce6ed4&sv=2)

# Downloads Manager | Adaptix Framework

The Downloads Tab displays all current or completed downloads.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FjsCu2HeSe8EhWLG0UkN3%252F52.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07070220-6b6e-4d7a-b63b-018b2ce66112&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f67f7bf4&sv=2)

The context menu provides options to cancel the download, as well as stop and resume the download.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FtQx7xgyIr2UAahiYhSXu%252F53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daed1de7b-3ee0-4def-ab95-5b003fe0473e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8eeb84b0&sv=2)

The downloaded files are stored on AdaptixServer. To copy a file from the server to the client system, select it and click "Sync file to client". Adaptix will then download the selected files to the folder on your system that you selected in the dialog box.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FOweMGJb9UjfGuV5V9uGO%252F54.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De04fda7a-0a98-483d-9a47-e924d2ef1e44&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=311fd2ac&sv=2)

# Linking Agents | Adaptix Framework

AdaptixC2 supports agent chains (linking agents). These linked agents receive their commands and send their output through the parent agent in their chain. This type of chaining is useful to control which sessions egress a network and to emulate a disciplined actor who restricts their communication paths inside of a network to something plausible.

For a linked agent, the External field will contain the parent agent ID and link name instead of the external IP address. Registered but not currently linked agents are marked as Unlink.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FmraoZhutN4PFCLXEOa0p%252FScreenshot_20251229_211625.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8460751-69fe-4b24-a40d-21fe09b5d641&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cf8ce333&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F4UcuHLAYzlHdPXwjYMln%252FScreenshot_20251229_211531.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a057e63-b9eb-4d08-95c2-73ca7bc7aabc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cdd7c9d5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/linking-agents#agents-that-support-the-linking-function)

Agent

SMB

[Beacon](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/beacon)

[Beacon TCP](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/listeners/beacon-tcp)

# Credentials Manager | Adaptix Framework

The Credentials Tab displays all stored credentials.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FtXdtuzqWadRQS8fCzrrb%252FScreenshot_20250728_181635.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71cfc370-5b23-42ac-9802-843090558f17&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6cc2efc6&sv=2)

The context menu provides the ability to create a new item, edit or delete an existing one.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FA7u0c2uukkOYoa5hzoWi%252FScreenshot_20251229_211127.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3b45ccbe-3317-4c00-ab36-625b71c74534&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=acc1cbcc&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FalaJ3khdC3SIm1PEEmPW%252FScreenshot_20250728_181702.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D838a326f-866a-49ed-b4ff-1f70ee0bd3da&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=25669e57&sv=2)

The **Export** menu allows you to export credentials in a specific format:

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F7ddgkeGneUw6RkjPlZAU%252FScreenshot_20251229_211144.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22a2f1e8-b823-45b2-8d14-4bb38d44cb39&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b894354f&sv=2)

`%realm%` - will be replaced by realm from credentials

`%username%` - will be replaced by username from credentials

`%password%` - will be replaced by password from credentials

# Installation Client | Adaptix Framework

The [source code arrow-up-right](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/AdaptixC2)
of AdaptixС2 is available on github. The `main` branch is a stable version and does not contain the latest changes.

Copy

    git clone https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/AdaptixC2.git
    cd AdaptixC2

* * *

Requires **QT > 6.8.0**, otherwise use docker.

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-client#preinstall)

Preinstall

To build Client, you need to install additional dependencies

Auto

Manual

For Linux (no Arch), you can use a specially prepared script that will install and configure the necessary packages for both the server and client parts. ([pre\_install\_linux\_all.sharrow-up-right](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Adaptix-Framework/AdaptixC2/refs/heads/main/pre_install_linux_all.sh)
)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FdI5lYBqGTLcNVOHoQDTD%252FScreenshot_20251230_175836.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3798d7dd-a995-41c0-8a4b-f8e58ee42c71&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=adf0d8a&sv=2)

**Debian**

Copy

    sudo apt install gcc g++ build-essential make cmake mingw-w64 g++-mingw-w64 libssl-dev qt6-base-dev qt6-base-private-dev libxkbcommon-dev qt6-websockets-dev qt6-declarative-dev qt6-svg-dev 

**Arch**

Copy

    sudo pacman -S --needed make cmake openssl libxkbcommon qt6-base qt6-websockets qt6-declarative

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-client#build-on-host)

Build on Host

The AdaptixClient is compiled from the cmake configuration. For fast builds in multithreaded mode, use `make client-fast`.

AdaptixClient file will be located in the dist directory.

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-client#build-in-docker)

Build in Docker

The compiled static AppImage will be located in the `AdaptixClient/client-dist` directory.

.

The AdaptixClient is compiled from the cmake configuration. For fast builds in multithreaded mode, use `make client-fast`.

. AdaptixClient.exe file will be located in the `AdaptixClient\dist` directory.

The directory with the application and dependencies can be transferred to any computer.

# Tasks manager | Adaptix Framework

A task can be of two types:

*   TASK — a fast task, executed in a single-threaded mode, delaying all other agent functions.
    
*   JOB — a task executed in the background. As a rule, such a task is executed longer in a separate thread or process. BOF can also be executed.
    
*   TUNNEL — a task indicating the start or stop of network tunnels.
    

AdaptixС2 registers and saves in the database all tasks ever completed. The task table displays the task type, the operator who started the task, the time of task execution, its status and a short answer.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fvu9QyBBmzUMWDS9Z33Me%252FScreenshot_20250224_214344.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f967d38-0a6f-4d7a-8835-05e58baaeb3d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d12b7fa9&sv=2)

The output of a specific command is displayed in the Task Output console when you select a task in the Tasks table.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FY274AqSPwxyrnI70KcjB%252F47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d86285a-6a4c-4d51-93b9-96ddf57eb8e4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3b3a5a8e&sv=2)

To activate the search bar, you must use the key combination `Ctrl+F` in the task table.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FygkfKzB879POlsDinORP%252FScreenshot_20251229_212104.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D389bf1c9-f90d-4e64-8273-f7e51c24d346&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=20ebb484&sv=2)

The Tasks table has the ability to filter tasks by individual agents.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FoFe469S3bmNcqKMTr1CA%252FScreenshot_20251229_212117.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da27293e2-de73-44e1-9e95-4966bdb81d4c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=afaa60e1&sv=2)

Tasks can be filtered by status. For example, you can filter only cancelled tasks or only those that are in progress (convenient for Jobs).

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FpJwuZtN8gUHH7bVRRrNf%252FScreenshot_20251229_212141.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D052f78d5-d4eb-497b-a15f-8524a843680f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5330e453&sv=2)

The Task table has the ability to filter by a substring in a command or by the result of its execution.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FxtM9Uv5k2qqijhG0rpEO%252FScreenshot_20251229_212223.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D55a90322-3307-4474-a1f5-7d4ddacc4c7f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d6d64e60&sv=2)

The context menu provides options to terminate the currently running task, as well as delete tasks from the database. In addition, you can quickly copy the task ID or console command and immediately go to the console of the selected agent.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FI6ToSqMoyz6U6S2gp779%252F51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2caaed35-2f9f-432c-9366-031bf850fd93&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=13f425d3&sv=2)

# Gopher TCP | Adaptix Framework

"Gopher TCP" listener starts a tcp/mtls server and registers a "gopher" agent.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F2IrY86OwaVR4E00FITxS%252FScreenshot_20251229_201056.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24bc34d0-599b-4fa7-ad9a-e48acbb4c809&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=608e766e&sv=2)

Parameter

Description

**Host & port (Bind)**

**Required.** The interface address and port to which your TCP Gopher server will bind.

**Callback addresses**

**Required.** List of address:port to which the agent will send requests. Current server rotation strategy: round-robin.

**Timeout (sec)**

The time to wait between connections in the event of a connection failure or interruption

**TCP banner**

Data that the server will send when any client connects to the port

**Error answer**

Server response if agent is not registered

**Encryption key**

Communication channel encryption key

**Use mTLS**

If set, use mTLS. Certificates and keys are not generated on the server

**How to Generate Certificates and Keys for mTLS**

[PreviousBeacon TCPchevron-left](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/listeners/beacon-tcp)
[NextAgentschevron-right](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents)

Last updated 3 months ago

Copy

    # CA cert
    openssl genrsa -out ca.key 2048
    openssl req -x509 -new -nodes -key ca.key -sha256 -days 3650 -out ca.crt -subj "/CN=Test CA"
    
    # server cert and key
    openssl genrsa -out server.key 2048
    openssl req -new -key server.key -out server.csr -subj "/CN=localhost"
    openssl x509 -req -in server.csr -CA ca.crt -CAkey ca.key -CAcreateserial -out server.crt -days 365 -sha256
    
    # client cert and key
    openssl genrsa -out client.key 2048
    openssl req -new -key client.key -out client.csr -subj "/CN=client"
    openssl x509 -req -in client.csr -CA ca.crt -CAkey ca.key -CAcreateserial -out client.crt -days 365 -sha256

# Targets Manager | Adaptix Framework

The Targets Tab displays all stored targets.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FzyrOTuQ86LUZxmAl6GeE%252FScreenshot_20250828_132020.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6de63a92-962c-456d-8a44-c4a5513ad412&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8adf1f9b&sv=2)

The context menu provides the ability to create a new item, edit or delete an existing one.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FWqZlcBgebOc0zK6MONGo%252FScreenshot_20251229_210923.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D176bc535-e2fa-43c5-9041-ade570211563&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e424739f&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FjgYkCokspkOVAHuqzfMt%252FScreenshot_20250828_132442.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f83dd25-3a02-4297-9939-19f3f9393227&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=54727248&sv=2)

The **Export** menu allows you to export targets in a specific format:

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FQwAylLpLzAUUVWYAlRln%252FScreenshot_20250828_132458.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De63f4a21-a7c6-487a-95ea-70012372358b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d4675fad&sv=2)

`%computer%` - will be replaced by computer from targets

`%domain%` - will be replaced by domain from targets

`%address%` - will be replaced by `address` from targets

# Tunnels and Forwarding | Adaptix Framework

AdaptixC2 provides the ability to use several pivot options. For each of these options, you need to make sure that yours agent supports a specific feature and is in interactive mode (sleep 0). By default, the agent is not put into interactive mode.

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/tunnels-and-forwarding#create-tunnels)

Create tunnels

Create a tunnel using the **Create Tunnel** context menu of the session table or graph if the agent supports one of the tunnel types.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F5VdviQJ77N9wsHjJ5Lu9%252FScreenshot_20250727_223330.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dde6e74b0-088d-4390-9f15-3cc70a640caa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e75e72a3&sv=2)

AdaptixC2 supports the following types of network tunnels:

*   SOCKS4
    
*   SOCKS5 (with/out Auth) TCP/UDP (IPv4, DNS, **not IPv6**)
    
*   Local TCP Port Forwarding
    
*   Reverse TCP Port Forwarding
    

Socks5

Socks4

Local port Forwarding

Reverse port Forwarding

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F00sBqyr0gR0UcSEtm4nG%252FScreenshot_20250528_133227.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1632792c-fa25-4769-8a92-6cb0d11123d0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=38eb333a&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FoABv8Y0s6moHLyi5WRtJ%252FScreenshot_20250528_133233.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8aaef832-b913-4032-a3d7-f51377705bdc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1984f36&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FbrMqNKvY9lE8zaJLwMxK%252FScreenshot_20250528_133238.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D669d0d01-86e9-4892-abd1-88264559f9f1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4c2815c0&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FuKv7Mfx6GbvlEGazcqGl%252FScreenshot_20250528_133244.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Defd69026-a64b-4ab0-949b-f59903ea9d3b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3b6eac2&sv=2)

AdaptixC2 allows you to build tunnels not only through the C2 teamserver (route: `-> C2 -> agent -> target`), but also through AdaptixClient.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fj7vglFRkjQUSwJ3m0YXW%252FScreenshot_20250528_133325.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D07de4f87-03a5-46d5-a21a-dd51a18fb1a5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9e10796d&sv=2)

In this case, the port is opened on the client and the traffic is directed along the path: `-> Client -> C2 -> agent -> target`.

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/tunnels-and-forwarding#tunnel-manager)

Tunnel manager

Created tunnels are managed via the tunnel manager.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FI1tAvuvvA6imHhl4jz8l%252FScreenshot_20250225_001926.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9befa7b-7b83-4448-bb67-51de1efff2bc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d6a3a0d7&sv=2)

The context menu of the Tunnels Table allows you to set information about the tunnel and stop the tunnel.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F2IrfdNH65KfvHiFIceFI%252FScreenshot_20250225_001938.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7afa1c9e-6c7c-4ab9-baa7-33c1934c436e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=590068f9&sv=2)

circle-info

Management of tunnels running through a client is available only to the user through whose client the tunnel is running
