# v1.0 -> v1.1 | Adaptix Framework

circle-info

Contributors to the GitHub update include: [shashinmaarrow-up-right](https://github.com/shashinma)
, [AnvithLoboarrow-up-right](https://github.com/AnvithLobo)
, [LongWayHomiearrow-up-right](https://github.com/LongWayHomie)
, [nth347arrow-up-right](https://github.com/nth347)
, [newBBnewarrow-up-right](https://github.com/newBBnew)
, [lesteratSOLarrow-up-right](https://github.com/lesteratSOL)
, [BlackMeerkatarrow-up-right](https://github.com/BlackMeerkat)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/v1.0-greater-than-v1.1#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   The data synchronization model has been completely redesigned. Data categories and category subscriptions have been introduced. Now, when logging in and during work, operators can select which data to synchronize.
    

Login subscriptions

Runtime subscriptions

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FEgnatOaKtsKFj1U0rNws%252FScreenshot_20260129_105805.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dca40d8c4-71cd-4f33-80f3-90b108ffe12e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5928e401&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FAVvwq1Lx6iN5rqqgRym8%252FScreenshot_20260129_105826.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D039d0406-ca9b-4519-8366-9094d389954b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8c403f82&sv=2)

*   Completely redesigned extenders models.
    
*   Agent generation can now be performed in a separate channel, allowing build status to be displayed online and without being affected by timeouts.
    
*   Agents now have a `multi_listeners mode`, which can be configured in the extender configuration. This mode allows you to generate an agent that will work with an unlimited number of listeners simultaneously, regardless of their protocol.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FUh2w9HCy27JUQeT0SKTN%252FScreenshot_20260130_114842.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D616bfdcf-bc75-4fcb-824e-ca5c8ed0a7d3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7f426f7a&sv=2)

*   YAML is now used to store configurations instead of JSON.
    
*   The main HTTP server of the team server now has the ability to flexibly configure HTTP connection parameters.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fr8e6ZOEpn8eVA8NNQ0Sv%252FScreenshot_20260130_115040.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd24a6b9-d7d3-4077-ba8b-a118cb907098&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1f7a4bc6&sv=2)

*   The tunnels have been improved and optimized (by [AnvithLoboarrow-up-right](https://github.com/AnvithLobo)
    )
    
*   Columns in the session table can now be moved. Columns now automatically adjust to the correct size (by [newBBnewarrow-up-right](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    
*   Now the listener state (paused or running) is saved and restored from the database.
    
*   Adds new themes: Adaptix Dracula, Dark Ice, Glass Morphism, Hacker Tech (by [newBBnewarrow-up-right](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    
*   New AxScript functions:
    
    *   Menu: `menu.add_main`, `menu.add_main_project`, `menu.add_main_axscript`, `menu.add_main_settings`.
        
    *   Ax: `ax.file_dirname`, `ax.file_extension`, `ax.file_size`, `ax.file_write_binary`, `ax.decode_data`, `ax.decode_file`, `ax.encode_data`, `ax.encode_file`, `ax.convert_to_code`, `ax.get_prject`.
        
    

**Fix:**

*   The issue of re-saving an agent profile with a configuration already existing in the database has been resolved.
    
*   Fix duplicate remote shell writes in teamserver (by [BlackMeerkatarrow-up-right](https://github.com/BlackMeerkat)
    )
    
*   Reverse Port Forwarding errors have been fixed (by [AnvithLoboarrow-up-right](https://github.com/AnvithLobo)
    )
    

* * *

Gopher


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   The Gopher agent profile now supports `multi_listeners` mode. This means that multiple different listeners can be configured for the agent, regardless of protocol.

    )

templates-extender


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   A new task type has been introduced: TASK\_TYPE\_LOCAL. This task type is used to retrieve information and returns the task output directly to the client; it is not saved to the database or sent to agents or other clients.
    
*   The agent config now has a `multi_listeners` parameter.

# Beacon SMB | Adaptix Framework

"Beacon SMB" is an internal listener used to communicate with the "Beacon" agent over SMB named pipes.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F95YKiQ7KxEUMFdPqu82i%252FScreenshot_20251229_201042.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8541145f-f3ea-4b4d-bd92-f04359d1b45c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a034a02&sv=2)

# v0.9 -> v0.10 | Adaptix Framework

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.9-greater-than-v0.10#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   **Sessions Table data model updated.** Eliminates small per-second UI stutters when many sessions are present.
    
*   **Tasks Manager data model updated.** Server synchronization is now orders of magnitude faster; loading, searching and filtering saved tasks complete in sub-second time.
    
*   **Credentials Manager data model updated.** Server sync and local data operations (read/filter) are dramatically faster.
    
*   **Targets Manager data model updated.** Synchronization and data handling significantly accelerated.
    
*   **Last column behavior changed:** if an agent has not checked in for more than 24 hours, the **Last** column shows the timestamp of the agent’s last check-in.
    
*   **Non-blocking server API calls:** API requests no longer block the main UI thread (by [newBBnewarrow-up-right](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    
*   **Cloudflare Tunnels support** added (by [newBBnewarrow-up-right](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    
*   **TLS 1.2–1.3** support added (by [newBBnewarrow-up-right](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )
    
*   **Client–server log sync optimized** using batch processing to improve throughput and reduce overhead (by [lsr00terarrow-up-right](https://github.com/lsr00ter)
    )
    

**Fix:**

*   **Tunnel handling fix:** a regression in the previous release broke task processing, which caused tunnels via linked agents to fail and made tunnels through external listeners unstable. This is now fixed.
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.9-greater-than-v0.10#beacon)

Beacon


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Service messages during BOF execution are no longer spammed; the console now logs only BOF start/end events and error messages.
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.9-greater-than-v0.10#extension-kit)

Extension-Kit


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   `smartscan` added to SAR-BOF (by [newBBnewarrow-up-right](https://github.com/newBBnew)
    )

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FfHApVwYsEsBkdXlLAQTT%252FScreenshot_20251029_222319.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb0c2b0c-fbed-4eaa-ba9d-2abf5f2aa15e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8e2e0d4c&sv=2)

*   `poolparty`: fixed ALPC port name randomization to prevent beacon crashes with certain injection techniques (by [jacopoaugelliarrow-up-right](https://github.com/jacopoaugelli)
    )
    
*   `ldapsearch`: LDAP signing/sealing implementation fixed.
    
*   `ldapsearch`**:** use DC hostname instead of IP for LDAP connections.
    
*   `cacls`**:** fixed out-of-bounds error.
    
*   `token make`**:** added support for multi-language usernames.

# Version 1.0 | Adaptix Framework

circle-exclamation

The client and server database structures have been changed and are not backward compatible with previous versions.

circle-info

Contributors to the GitHub update include: [shashinmaarrow-up-right](https://github.com/shashinma)
, [P0142arrow-up-right](https://github.com/P0142)
, [bri5eearrow-up-right](https://github.com/bri5ee)
, [BlackMeerkatarrow-up-right](https://github.com/BlackMeerkat)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/version-1.0#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Network tunnels SOCKS4/SOCKS5 have been completely reworked on both client and server sides, significantly improving stability, performance, and speed. Tunnels are now RFC-compliant, which allows port scanning through tunnels. SOCKS5 tunnels (both client-side and server-side) now support IPv6 (Client and TeamServer). Added an internal TeamServer API for service responses to the SOCKS client about connection status: `TsTunnelConnectionHalt(channelId int, errorCode byte)`
    
*   The session graph has been completely redesigned. New icons have been added. Support for Top-Bottom layout has been introduced. Sessions through which tunnels are operating are now marked as TunS (tunnel via TeamServer) and TunC (tunnel via client). Inactive and Terminated sessions are no longer displayed on the graph. Quick session console opening via mouse middle-click.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FP9DKARFpkY5yaF4TKWx8%252FScreenshot_20251229_225406.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D44c8175b-cf3e-4d76-a08f-48fd4facf203&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1480ac6c&sv=2)

*   Dialog windows have been reworked and a profile system with background saving to the client database has been added for: Authorization Form, Listener Creation Window, Agent Generation Window. The authorization form now requires specifying a project directory, which will be used as the base path for all file system dialogs.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F48XLkIdBfPj28Pj3QSlB%252FScreenshot_20251229_204213.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daac4f74e-8139-4ae9-b3a3-94e19847be63&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3f7b51e7&sv=2)

*   Implemented Remote Shell — an interactive Non-PTY shell. This required rewriting the API `TsTerminalConnResume(agentId, terminalId, ioDirect bool)`.
    
*   Remote Terminal now operates in SSH-like mode (fast input + stable PTY). Multiple terminals can now be created within a single Remote Terminal tab.
    

Term 1

Term2

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fegld7ifphDuWDNAbzz5p%252FScreenshot_20251229_220225.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05295ca9-49b1-48a7-bc90-18bc29e56f6d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=81691a1b&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FaDsFMwPvMVjgbooZYWUv%252FScreenshot_20251229_220230.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc816268f-a3e3-44fb-bcb4-a8f9a42af3ff&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b458afd9&sv=2)

*   The client now interacts with the server using asynchronous functions
    
*   AxScript is now executed asynchronously if the script does not use UI elements
    
*   A Handler mechanism for commands executed via AxScript has been implemented using new Ax APIs: [execute\_alias](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_alias)
    , [execute\_alias\_hook](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_alias)
    , [execute\_alias\_handler](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_alias)
    , [execute\_command](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_command)
    , [execute\_command\_hook](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_command)
    , [execute\_command\_handler](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_command)
    
*   When a command is entered incorrectly, the help output is now displayed by default.
    
*   Added the ability to modify session parameters via the context menu
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FKVqsae4dOJ19np9J9gkP%252FScreenshot_20251229_223727.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De5ab1deb-3fb4-49b9-9304-06868b1eb380&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=77b7fa49&sv=2)

*   Added tab blinking animation for background updates (by [shashinmaarrow-up-right](https://github.com/shashinma))
    )
    
*   Added the ability to rename tabs via the context menu (by [shashinmaarrow-up-right](https://github.com/shashinma))
    )
    
*   Tabs can now be closed by middle-clicking the tab or using a three-finger touchpad gesture
    
*   Added text batching to prevent UI freezes: flush every 100 ms or 64 KB, optimized bulk line removal, and added a database truncation limit of 10 MB (by [bri5eearrow-up-right](https://github.com/bri5ee)
    )
    
*   The Listener Manager now includes a Created column with the listener creation date and time
    
*   The Sessions table now includes a Created column with the agent creation date and time
    
*   Targets Manager now supports copying data to the clipboard
    
*   Credentials Manager now supports copying data to the clipboard. When copying credentials, templates can now be selected (impacket, netexec, etc.)
    
*   DownloadsManager now allows deleting multiple saved files at once
    
*   In all tables, Ctrl+F now enables filtering and searching. The search field supports conditional operators: `and` &, `or` |, `not` ^, `grouping` ().
    
*   The client synchronization system has been updated
    
*   Added new themes: Adaptix Dark and Adaptix Light

Ax Light

*   Added Slack event callbacks.
    
*   Implemented global managers: TaskManager, TunnelManager, EventBroker.
    
*   Added Docker Compose build commands to the Makefile.

*   Removed Web API
    

**Fix:**

*   Authorization errors on the Windows client have been resolved
    
*   Correct handling of `PostHook` even when the client is disconnected
    
*   Fixed an issue with automatic titlebar enlargement (by [shashinmaarrow-up-right](https://github.com/shashinma)
    )
    
*   Fixed buttons and centering issues in the tabbar and titlebar (by [shashinmaarrow-up-right](https://github.com/shashinma)
    )
    
*   Fixed date sorting in all tables
    
*   Fixed Console UI freezing when displaying large outputs (by [bri5eearrow-up-right](https://github.com/bri5ee)
    )
    
*   Fixed focus restoration so tabs no longer auto-switch when agents connect (by [bri5eearrow-up-right](https://github.com/bri5ee)
    )
    
*   Fixed an issue where port 1080 was always used when creating SOCKS4 tunnels from the UI
    
*   On client reconnect, if the server is still unavailable, the synchronization banner is now hidden automatically

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    )

    )
    
*   Increased `cat` command output size from 10 KB to 1 MB.

# Beacon HTTP | Adaptix Framework

"Beacon HTTP" listener starts a web server and registers a "beacon" agent.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FVBwxuloLwUmWRvwZ31rd%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0_20260228_213713.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab058a4e-9d12-4889-8836-a170dcf7122f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3378155c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/listeners/beacon-http#beacon-http-parameters)

Beacon HTTP parameters


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Main settings

HTTP Headers

Page Error

Page Payload

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FxFSatVezavlv0Gu3NbbS%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0_20260228_213727.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De52a9ee3-c066-4c0d-9e8e-7d627c449815&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=41360699&sv=2)

Parameter

Description

**Host & port (Bind)**

**Required.** The interface address and port to which your HTTP Beacon web server will bind.

**Callback addresses**

**Required.** List of address:port to which the agent will send requests. Current server rotation strategy: round-robin.

**Method**

The HTTP method that the agent will use to transmit data to the server and receive commands

**URI**

**Required.** The HTTP endpoint to which the agent sends the request.

**User-Agent**

**Required.** User-Agent for HTTP requests

**Heartbeat Header**

**Required.** The HTTP header in which the agent will transmit registration information

**Encryption key**

**Required.** Communication channel encryption key

**Use SSL**

If set, use HTTPS. If the SSL certificate and key are not specified, the server will generate them itself.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FTdiadVyDhGtfKXnUBqxE%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0_20260228_213730.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24c5c6d5-98f2-4c8b-b033-dbb160512145&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=103193ba&sv=2)

Parameter

Description

**Trust X-Forwarded-For**

This option decides if listener uses the X-Forwarded-For HTTP header to determine the remote address of a request. _Use this option if your AdaptixServer is behind an HTTP redirector_

**Host Header**

Host header for HTTP requests

Request Headers

HTTP headers that the agent will use when sending the request

Server Headers

HTTP headers that will be in the server's response.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FLX6CPrEf1DxqCRqyufUB%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0_20260228_213734.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da9377252-007f-445c-9a88-5d3d4973265a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56c7d856&sv=2)

**Page Error** \- the HTTP server's response to any request that is not from an agent.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FhC9LJs245QVZ2hEvuBcS%252F%25D0%25A1%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B8%25D0%25BC%25D0%25BE%25D0%25BA%2520%25D1%258D%25D0%25BA%25D1%2580%25D0%25B0%25D0%25BD%25D0%25B0_20260228_213736.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da93393a8-8fde-4b1f-96ae-2604b74fbe83&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dc64c6cb&sv=2)

**Page Payload** - Server response to agent request. `<<<PAYLOAD_DATA>>>` will be replaced with data for the agent.

[PreviousListenerschevron-left](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/listeners)
[NextBeacon DNSchevron-right](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/listeners/beacon-dns)

Last updated 1 month ago

# Beacon TCP | Adaptix Framework

The "Beacon TCP" uses a TCP socket to communicate through a parent Beacon agent. This peer-to- peer communication works with Beacons on the same host and across the network.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Ff5nVv18cufTfNQHH13Ws%252FScreenshot_20251229_201048.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc4210137-9956-4f03-8b12-1aa89c4c06fe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=687fb0f0&sv=2)

*   **Bind port —** Default TCP Beacon listen port
    
*   **Prepend data —** Prepend header to TCP Beacon messages
    
*   **Enctyption key —** Communication channel encryption key
    

[PreviousBeacon SMBchevron-left](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/listeners/beacon-smb)
[NextGopher TCPchevron-right](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/listeners/gopher-tcp)

Last updated 3 months ago

# v0.2 -> v0.3 | Adaptix Framework

circle-info

If you previously used **AdaptixClient**, delete the `~/.adaptix/storage.db` file.

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.2-greater-than-v0.3#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   The session table now has agent markings: Terminated, Inactive, Unlink, No response. The operator can mark an agent as Inactive or Active, and also select the color of the entry or the entire line. The time for marking an agent as No Response is set in the session table settings. The User field now displays the access token used. Icons have appeared in the OS field.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F09Uh2sMREfzMBsGO5ucG%252FScreenshot_20250327_162107.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D394074b9-82d4-4229-946b-96684f0f4fd3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6bb3549&sv=2)

*   Session graph added to AdaptixClient. The server implements interfaces for "internal" listeners (eg SMB listener).
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FuvESFwkQgqk4vTWOFK4H%252FScreenshot_20250327_162134.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D09824ae7-9694-422e-9409-813ff1248bb1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9afe611f&sv=2)

*   When deleting an agent from the server via the "Remove from server" menu item through the session table menu, you now need to confirm the action.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fm4HOeysZ5Q29ZHNzI03H%252FScreenshot_20250327_163010.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf5440fb-2643-4b10-8248-3efdb7bca5e1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=99d4392b&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FjhmfYZcmkq0NlfQQi95l%252FScreenshot_20250327_163020.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D06c4f660-7ceb-4e32-9697-77838f9421f7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=345285d7&sv=2)

*   Added the User field to TasksTable. Also, all tasks now have one of the statuses: Hosted, Running, Completed. Reworked server interfaces for working with TaskData and console output, added a new task type - TYPE\_PROXY\_DATA. Extension developers received a more flexible task management mechanism.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FjIVYOFSlhVY1UhdY1U6t%252FScreenshot_20250327_162859.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd27781cd-6cc9-4b0b-bcb0-24b2d96bf239&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2fcc953d&sv=2)

*   Added search panels to SessionsTable and TaskTable. To activate the panel, use the `Ctrl+F` key combination in the table.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FNb1Rnfhet3IabmKLozwo%252FScreenshot_20250327_144957.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D14297206-fd44-49d6-9866-953f8b31e19c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7376ff&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FvWysdSgH8yFlj2vDCqsD%252FScreenshot_20250327_145553.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D488b23a2-e76b-4588-be28-f9c469cb7a8e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5d61e22&sv=2)

*   Now, when synchronizing with the server, tasks in TasksTable will be sorted by creation time, and not by agent ID
    
*   Now when synchronizing with the server, agents in SessionsTable will be synchronized by creation time, and not by agent ID
    
*   Arguments in `help` are now displayed in formatted form.
    
*   Changed the appearance of the listener and agent creation windows (the load and save buttons have been moved to the top)
    
*   An interface for handling agent shutdown has been added to the server.
    
*   Golang packages updated from go-1.22 to go-1.23
    
*   Added docker build (by [ArchiMoebiusarrow-up-right](https://github.com/ArchiMoebius)
    )
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed a bug in the client with packing BYTES for translation to BOF (by [ArturLukianovarrow-up-right](https://github.com/ArturLukianov)
    )
    
*   Fixed a client bug where information was being written to the wrong field in DownloadsTable (by [uxbugarrow-up-right](https://github.com/uxbug)
    )
    
*   Now when you close the main client window, all open windows are closed and the application exits
    
*   The main menu now works correctly in KDE panel widgets
    
*   Compliter in the agent console no longer requires additional confirmation if the text was entered manually. Duplication for commands with subcommands has been removed
    
*   On the server, situations have been fixed where the information of the last loaded module overwrote the information of previously loaded modules
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.2-greater-than-v0.3#agent-beacon)

Agent Beacon


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Added SMB communication channel
    
*   Added `rev2self`, `getuid`, `link`, and `unlink` commands
    
*   Sensitive strings are hidden in the agent
    
*   The service name is no longer present inside DLL, EXE, and Shellcode type agents
    
*   Added BOF API: `BeaconIsAdmin`
    
*   Added Chinese language support for coders (by [HongLuDianXuearrow-up-right](https://github.com/HongLuDianXue)
    )
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed memory accumulation in `ProcessDownloadTasks` (by [M1ndoarrow-up-right](https://github.com/M1ndo)
    )
    
*   Fixed memory leaks, no more accumulation of allocated memory
    
*   The ls command now displays the correct last modification time of files
    
*   Now when creating a listener, the value of the `Port Callback` field is validated
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.2-greater-than-v0.3#extension-kit)

    )
    
*   SAR-BOF: `quser` (by [B1oodyPhoenixarrow-up-right](https://github.com/B1oodyPhoenix)
    )
    
*   SAL-BOF: `arp`, `cacls`, `dir`, `env`, `ipconfig`, `listdns`, `netstat`, `nslookup`, `routerprint`, `uptime`, `useridletime`, `whoami` (by [B1oodyPhoenixarrow-up-right](https://github.com/B1oodyPhoenix)
    )
    
*   LateralMovement-BOF: `token_make` и `token_steal`
    
*   Elevation-BOF: `getsystem_token`
    
*   Injection-BOF: `inject-sec`

# v0.10 -> v0.11 | Adaptix Framework

circle-exclamation

Go version has been updated from 1.24.4 to 1.25.4, so **a full installation** [**following the guide**](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-server#preinstall)
 **is required**.

circle-info

Contributed to this update: [shashinmaarrow-up-right](https://github.com/shashinma)
, [cr0eaxarrow-up-right](https://github.com/cr0eax)
, [Xre0uSarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
, [M1ndoarrow-up-right](https://github.com/M1ndo)
, [ArturLukianovarrow-up-right](https://github.com/ArturLukianov)
, [entropy-zarrow-up-right](https://github.com/entropy-z)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.10-greater-than-v0.11#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Golang has been updated from version 1.24.4 to 1.25.4. The new version will use the new experimental `encoding/json/v2` package and the new experimental `greenteagc` garbage collector.
    
*   Synchronization of extension package versions and the framework itself is now controlled by a single `go work` statement.
    
*   The synchronization mechanism has been optimized. The entire client interface is now blocked during synchronization.
    
*   The `GenerateUI` function in axscript now also returns the `ui_height` and `ui_width` properties, which adjust the window for creating listeners or agents.
    
*   Client UI: Add dynamic title bar styling based on theme (by [shashinmaarrow-up-right](https://github.com/shashinma)
    )
    
*   Added building server and extenders in [docker compose](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-server#docker-compose)
     (by [shashinmaarrow-up-right](https://github.com/shashinma)
    )
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed errors with interrupted upload and synchronization of large files.
    
*   Fixed an issue where the sync progress bar would not appear when reconnecting to the server.
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.10-greater-than-v0.11#beacon)

Beacon


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Classes that store this during initialization will get pointer to temporary memory (on stack) because of current construction method. Code changed to use new/delete with overridden operator new/operator delete for each of beacon class. (by [cr0eaxarrow-up-right](https://github.com/cr0eax)
    )
    

**Fix**:

*   Problem in `BeaconFormatPrintf`/`BeaconPrintf` because `vsnprintf` returns -1 on error which is later used as size leading to crash (by [cr0eaxarrow-up-right](https://github.com/cr0eax)
    )
    
*   Problem in `BeaconAddValue` and family. It stores `Char*` as raw pointer inside `Map<CHAR*, LPVOID> Values;` Changed to store actual key value (by [cr0eaxarrow-up-right](https://github.com/cr0eax)
    )
    
*   Ntdll `RtlRandomEx`, `RtlGetVersion` `__stdcall` for x86 (crash on shifted stack) (by [cr0eaxarrow-up-right](https://github.com/cr0eax)
    )
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.10-greater-than-v0.11#gopher)

Gopher


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   Golang has been updated from version 1.24.4 to 1.25.4.
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed an issue where the agent would not have a delay between reconnections.
    
*   The `cat` command now has a 10 KB limit.
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.10-greater-than-v0.11#extension-kit)

Extension-Kit


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   AD-BOF: Added `readlaps` BOF (by [Xre0uSarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Xre0uS)
    )

# BOF and Extensions | Adaptix Framework

circle-info

Official extensions: [https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/Extension-Kitarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/Extension-Kit)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#beacon-object-files)

Beacon Object Files


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BOF is just a block of position-independent code that receives pointers to some Beacon internal APIs. BOFs are single-file C programs that call Win32 APIs and limited [Beacon APIsarrow-up-right](https://hstechdocs.helpsystems.com/manuals/cobaltstrike/current/userguide/content/topics/beacon-object-files_bof-c-api.htm)
.

AdaptixC2 expects that your BOFs are single-threaded programs that run for a short period of time. BOFs will block other agent tasks and functionality from executing. BOFs execute inside of your agent. If a BOF crashes, you will lose access. Write your BOFs carefully.

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#description-of-bof-for-agents)

Description of BOF for agents

[Beacon BOFschevron-right](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/beacon/beacon-bofs)
[Gopher BOFschevron-right](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/gopher/gopher-bofs)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#extensions)

Extensions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[How to execute AxScriptchevron-right](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/how-to-execute-axscript)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FPVXLw0sNpy9JDkze8fti%252FScreenshot_20250724_194751.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De164eeab-6183-4695-8145-d74a92fe22dc&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fde902e0&sv=2)

The extension file is an AxScript that must start with a global definition of the metadata variable that has the following properties: .

*   `name` - extension name,
    
*   `description` - extension description
    
*   `store` - determines whether the extension should be stored in the database (default: `true`).
    

Typically, extensions register new commands to call already registered commands. An example of defining a `shell` command that calls the command `ps run -o ...`. [See more details here](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type)
.

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#axscript-and-bofs)

AxScript and BOFs


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You'll likely want to use AxScript to run your finalized BOF implementations within AdaptixC2. A BOF is a good place to implement a lateral movement technique, an escalation of privilege tool, or a new reconnaissance capability.

Each agent has its own command to execute BOF. For example, for a beacon agent it is `execute bof`. Here is a script to run a `screenshot_bof` BOF:

First, the script gets the `note` and `pid` values. The next step is to pack our arguments. The [bof\_pack](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axfunction#bof_pack)
 function packs arguments in a way that is compatible with Beacon's internal data parser API. This script uses [execute\_alias](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axcommand-type/commands-and-hooks#execute_alias)
 to run BOF with its arguments.

[PreviousScreenshots Managerchevron-left](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/data-management/screenshots-manager)
[NextTunnels and Forwardingchevron-right](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/tunnels-and-forwarding)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [Beacon Object Files](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#beacon-object-files)
    
*   [Description of BOF for agents](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#description-of-bof-for-agents)
    
*   [Extensions](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#extensions)
    
*   [AxScript and BOFs](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/bof-and-extensions#axscript-and-bofs)
    

Copy

    var metadata = {
        name: "Elevation-BOF",
        description: "BOFs for context elevation",
        store: true
    };
    
    // AxScript code
    // ...

Copy

    let cmd_shell = ax.create_command("shell", "Execute command via cmd.exe", "shell whoami /all");
    cmd_shell.addArgString("cmd_params", true);
    cmd_shell.setPreHook(function (id, cmdline, parsed_json, ...parsed_lines) {
        let new_cmd = "ps run -o C:\\Windows\\System32\\cmd.exe /c " + parsed_json["cmd_params"];
        ax.execute_alias(id, cmdline, new_cmd);
    });
    

Copy

    var cmd_screenshot = ax.create_command("screenshot_bof", "Alternative screenshot capability that does not do fork n run by @codex_tf2", "screenshot -n screen1 -p 812");
    cmd_screenshot.addArgFlagString("-n", "note", "Screenshot caption", "ScreenshotBOF");
    cmd_screenshot.addArgFlagInt("-p", "pid", "PID of the application whose window screenshot will be taken. If 0, then a full-screen screenshot", 0);
    cmd_screenshot.setPreHook(function (id, cmdline, parsed_json, ...parsed_lines) {
        let note = parsed_json["note"];
        let pid  = parsed_json["pid"];
    
        let bof_params = ax.bof_pack("cstr,int", [note, pid]);
        let bof_path = ax.script_dir() + "_bin/Screenshot." + ax.arch(id) + ".o";
    
        ax.execute_alias(id, cmdline, `execute bof ${bof_path} ${bof_params}`, "Task: Screenshot BOF");
    });

# User Interface | Adaptix Framework

The AdaptixClient user interface is divided into two main parts. The Session Table, Session Graph, and Tasks Manager widgets are initially docked in the upper part. The lower part contains tabs for each function you interact with.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FOKYspOwQrc2jrNGCby4E%252FScreenshot_20251229_204430.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da7a3f02d-8018-4f6d-a965-d239b52f2fd0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a25e0015&sv=2)

Each widget can be moved around in its Dock, grouped into Tabs, or undocked as a separate window.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F1B6aWVVxDmiuEB3XrMrQ%252FScreenshot_20250927_213254.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab0f5423-8d11-4bb3-97bd-c4eff8e478c1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7ebff42c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#main-menu)

Main menu


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#id-1.-projects)

1\. Projects

Project Management Menu. Close Project will disconnect the current project from the C2 server and close the project area. New Project will open a new login window.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FMFJKKU2Jis2nhzs1w7JE%252FScreenshot_20260128_223927.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc48b9f74-9135-43df-bdc3-a5b30596f5bf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=47c41da5&sv=2)

After authorization, a new project tab will appear in the bottom panel of the client. When you click on the folder icon, the project directory will open in the system explorer.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FiJB8Ue10clycWX2i41FQ%252FScreenshot_20260128_224000.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59668aa3-671e-4499-b52f-c5d007bfec0e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bce5ed09&sv=2)

The **Subscriptions** menu allows you to synchronize data that was not received during authorization.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FJ3eTFeoLVfhYhkaKXJHH%252FScreenshot_20260129_105826.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D12f30229-2c57-4ea1-b66d-f4de01ac6338&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c1afd861&sv=2)

Agent Console block allows you to set the default buffer size, as well as the console time display modes, line feeds, and auto-scroll to the last output.

Allows you to select which fields will be displayed in the [Sessions Table.](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#session-table)
 This section enables the HealthCheck feature and sets the agent monitoring time.

.

Toolbar


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The toolbar at the top of AdaptixClient offers quick access to common Adaptix functions.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FGWlE0HNEOLkcgM7IVtOe%252FScreenshot_20260128_224100.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a39da20-0658-4ccd-a127-84898ec43963&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3e0e6640&sv=2)

View Logs tab

Update JWT / Reconnect to Server

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#session-table)

Session Table


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The session table shows which agents have registered with the AdaptixServer.

The User field displays the access token used. The session table has agent markings: _Terminated_, _Inactive_, _Unlink_, _No response_. The operator can mark an agent as _Inactive_ or _Active_, and also select the color of the entry or the entire line. The time for marking an agent as _No Response_ is set in the session table settings.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fs3BewxSFOD9B4ghXUUkq%252FScreenshot_20250427_121831.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe718d6a-3e04-4fe3-aeb3-b6eb04e2cb9a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3a196218&sv=2)

Hovering over the Sleep field will show the current KillDate and WorkTime settings (if set). During non-working hours, the agent will be marked as "No worktime".

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fq6dnkHPxhUf2rNh1NSyi%252FScreenshot_20250427_222916.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddbab4ac0-e514-4156-a4d6-5d88615330f3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7ace57f6&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FM8r3q0I9enlktuGSnD2F%252FScreenshot_20250427_223011.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De17455c7-334a-423c-9dba-29643ce8cf44&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e1e6a52&sv=2)

Double-clicking on an agent line will open the agent console. Agents are managed via the context menu of the session table.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FkMK2ih6Wg71etkxGjnPH%252FScreenshot_20251229_223630.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db261a66f-a641-45a8-9240-4c59dbf89ace&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c0cc1c2&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F7i7EeAq3n3KI7HbAVyJO%252FScreenshot_20251229_223652.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D91e1dbcb-c613-4f19-afad-265398a1560b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a0b4cc94&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FXar1ptvPW9UWNdnPjgkm%252FScreenshot_20251229_223703.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8dac536-b57d-4001-b205-4473d6ab1547&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1eccf8c7&sv=2)

When deleting an agent from the server via the "Remove from server" menu item through the session table menu, you now need to confirm the action.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FcUNPLxBx40Z1nanVhSKe%252FScreenshot_20250327_163020.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df218c96d-088c-46ba-807f-124fcec26656&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c28ea2b7&sv=2)

"**Set data**" allows you to manually set session data.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FfXQJQJ3gvWJ8xH773i0B%252FScreenshot_20251229_223727.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dace6080a-464f-4251-82b3-f5addf696756&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=27926da9&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#search-and-filter)

Search and filter


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All tables support searching and filtering data. To display the search and filter bar, use the keyboard shortcut `Ctrl+F`.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fdv3VHgomg9rz3Jwhl4re%252FScreenshot_20251229_224113.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e505db3-928a-49ae-ac01-d41cc0bf89d5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89c6833b&sv=2)

The search field supports groupings and conditions:

*   `()` - group
    
*   `^()` - not
    
*   `|` - or
    
*   `&` - and.
    

If **auto** check is active, searching and filtering are performed online whenever the filter is changed. If **auto** check is disabled, searching and filtering are performed only by pressing Enter.

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#sessions-graph)

Sessions Graph


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Without a visual representation, it’s difficult to track and understand chains of 4 or 5 linked agents. That’s where the Sessions Graph comes in handy.

The session graph shows the agent chains in a natural way. Each agent session has a computer icon that indicates its operating system and privilege level. If the icon is red, the agent is running in a privileged process. A gray icon indicates that the agent is currently checked (possibly inactive).

The firewall icon represents the egress point of your agent. Each line contains the name of the listener responsible for processing agent data. A **dashed green line** indicates the use of "external" listeners.

A **solid yellow line** connecting one agent session to another represents a link between two agent ("internal" listener). These lines contain the listener name and the link name (e.g. `p0`).

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F51vghvWxFWRiZG4nKbTQ%252FScreenshot_20251229_211531.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc436e448-6ee4-44a8-b8b3-021eadd4c5ad&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=73d013f6&sv=2)

Agents are managed via the context menu of the session table.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F05hAFg4FLB36jjgFE5T5%252FScreenshot_20251229_224834.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b3da2bb-0737-4fda-9bab-6439467e9190&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=72c1df51&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FCF1bFA9sqz3RgKhCw1nG%252FScreenshot_20251229_224844.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc609c1b-d178-4420-8a0f-ebd8597f0dbf&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=630dc515&sv=2)

If a network tunnel is running through the agent, this will be shown in the graph.

*   TunS - teamserver-side
    
*   TunC - client-side
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FqMw3IC2f8bnnVrmi0WbZ%252FScreenshot_20251229_225406.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db91ca2e3-ed80-4e09-86e7-0c0c7711f311&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12e4ec01&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/user-interface#agents-console)

Agents console


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The agent console looks like this. Each command includes the operator name, task ID, and agent type.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fb5BEaXQNuR6zGpsQoi6m%252F20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D362d02c6-1858-440e-92b4-fa94abe6e16f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5f41deef&sv=2)

The console keeps a history of entered commands, as well as autocompletion of commands. The console supports auto-completion of local paths by pressing the `Tab` key, and `Ctrl+Tab` will open a file selection window. The console has its own menu with many settings.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FoAIfJtQTbL2ZLy8tFsYM%252FScreenshot_20250624_002120.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D58775a7b-a57e-402d-b2b0-110d789bc5be&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed751219&sv=2)

You can disable the display of time in the console in the application settings.

The console supports escaping quotes and slashes. An expression within the first quotation marks will be interpreted as a string for the console. If quotation marks need to be passed to a command, they must be escaped. An example of running mimikatz is below.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FRqT0DaVTszlNqQzyifrO%252FScreenshot_20251116_115807.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31c14803-ed01-4878-b364-37df6bb02771&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d85b8ed8&sv=2)

# v0.5 -> v0.6 | Adaptix Framework

circle-exclamation

Go version has been updated from 1.23.1 to 1.24.4, so **a full installation** [**following the guide**](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/getting-starting/installation-server#preinstall)
 **is required**.

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.5-greater-than-v0.6#adaptixc2)

AdaptixC2


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   **Agent Console – Path Autocompletion & File Selection Dialog.** Local file path autocompletion is now available in the agent console via the `Tab` key. Pressing `Ctrl+Tab` opens a **file selection dialog** for browsing the file system.
    
*   **Context Menu Enhancements (Agent Console & Logs Panel).** A context menu has been added to both the agent console and the Logs panel, allowing you to configure _AutoScroll_, _NoWrap_, and change the _console buffer size_ (limiting the number of lines). Default values for AutoScroll, NoWrap, and buffer size can be configured in Main Settings.
    
*   Search functionality (`Ctrl+F`) has been added to the agent console and the Logs panel.
    
*   Command history in the agent console is now restored upon synchronization with the server, even after client reconnection. Full history is available through the “Show History” context menu. Double-clicking a command in Show History inserts it into the input field.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FmkXmVRntMsnYHXx47vEg%252FScreenshot_20250624_002427.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debb605d4-039a-41d0-a980-733173b37fc4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=586fb52a&sv=2)

*   In **RemoteTerminal**, buffer size (line count) can now be configured via the context menu. The default value can be set in Main Settings.
    
*   **EventCallback** to Telegram BOT. More...
    
*   **New UI Theme and Font Support**. A new _Dracula_ theme has been added to AdaptixClient. It can be selected in client settings. Font support for _DejaVu Sans Mono_ and _Hack_ has been extended. New fonts _Space Mono_ and _Anonymous Pro_ have been added.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FFVk2xQleAQU3cbypmkoH%252FScreenshot_20250624_002057.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0568e8f-9793-4f38-bf6e-b56f352450f5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a90d1c99&sv=2)

*   The columns _Domain_, _Computer_, and _User_ in SessionsTable can now be resized manually.
    
*   **Enhanced Session Table Menu.** The session table menu has been redesigned. It is now possible to execute a command on multiple agents via the **'Agent' → 'Execute command'** menu. Console content can be permanently deleted via **'Agent' → 'Remove console data'**, while all tasks remain in TasksManager.
    
*   An additional graph version has been added (by [mil4nearrow-up-right](https://github.com/mil4ne)
    ). You can select which version to use in client settings.
    

Version 1

Verison 2

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fqon6CsftqH2HhGo8ZsH6%252FScreenshot_20250624_000616.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D413e973a-c30f-437d-951c-019aadc8551c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=83375a08&sv=2)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FEP1Ej9opE50ur4sfi1oJ%252FScreenshot_20250624_000636.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6cb25e2-6045-4928-8373-1e32eba188d8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c8b9414c&sv=2)

*   All settings are now applied in real time and no longer require a client restart.
    
*   **One-Time Password (OTP) Token System**. An OTP token system has been added for one-time access to objects. The endpoint `/otp/get` accepts the object type and its identifier (e.g. type: download, id: FileId). With the received token, you can access the `/download/sync/otp` endpoint and download a file once without authentication on the team server. Tasks larger than 5 MB are now uploaded as files using OTP. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/data-management/downloads-manager)
    
*   Synchronization of large files from DownloadsTable has been implemented. Files are uploaded through the client in a separate thread. A new window shows synchronization status and speed. You can also obtain an OTP and download the file via Curl or Wget. [More...](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/adaptix-c2/data-management/downloads-manager)
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FzhMZODwqDae5SC0ApjWw%252FScreenshot_20250624_000922.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28a54e42-eb7f-442c-9abe-ec224ac815e6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8ef7c75e&sv=2)

*   When restoring agents from the database, the client log now shows the date and time the agent was created.
    
*   The C2 endpoint may now contain the "." character.
    
*   Project structure has been refactored. Client build time has been reduced by approximately 50%.
    
*   Server has been updated from Go 1.23.1 to Go 1.24.4.
    

**Fix:**

*   Fixed an [issuearrow-up-right](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/AdaptixC2/issues/82)
     with incorrect task data validation. The client would terminate when executing a sequence of commands involving `file upload` and Beacon `agent termination`.
    
*   Fixed an issue with caching unsynchronized tasks. These tasks are no longer stored in server memory unless they are JOBs.
    
*   When copying Cmdline from TasksBrowser, an incorrect column value was copied. Now dynamic column indices are used.
    
*   Fixed color inconsistencies in the agent console when pasting previously copied data. The agent console no longer uses HTML for text formatting.
    
*   Fixed padding in UI styles. Buttons and input fields now have equal height.
    

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/changelog-and-updates/version-0.1-greater-than-1.0/v0.5-greater-than-v0.6#agent-beacon)

Agent Beacon


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**New:**

*   In the BeaconSMB listener, pipe names can now contain "." characters.
    
*   The `ps list` command now displays processes as a tree structure.
    

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FpWFpGOZwzsgJDfHK1YEQ%252FScreenshot_20250624_002639.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6daf2674-5655-444c-a10a-c0f812f4adfe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=572b34a5&sv=2)

    )
    
*   Added support for legacy Windows systems, including Windows 7 and Windows Server 2003 (by [yinselarrow-up-right](https://github.com/yinsel)

# Gopher | Adaptix Framework

triangle-exclamation

This version of the Gopher agent is not designed for AV or EDR evasion and is therefore not OPSEC compliant. Gopher is primarily intended to test and demonstrate the capabilities of AdaptixC2. However, the Gopher agent can be easily extended and modified, making it compatible with various AV evasion methods.

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/gopher#configuration)

Configuration


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252F4YzYFL2gSY9SOIzkqXT1%252FScreenshot_20260128_230718.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daf02dd93-f384-483e-ae38-6f1baece814f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a9a2c9b5&sv=2)

Gopher can work with several listeners at once, changing them if the current transport is unavailable. Gopher currently **supports Windows, Linux and MacOS**. The Gopher can be generated **for amd64 and arm64** architectures.

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/gopher#commands)

Commands


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Gopher currently supports the following commands.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FXCLqdNoKcTHTQOZQoKA5%252FScreenshot_20250427_215852.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5bce04f8-b6c4-4ca0-9f22-ca1f05aafb91&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e6a9db8e&sv=2)

The **download** and **run** commands create a new parallel connection. The **job kill** command can stop the download or execution of a command/script.

[PreviousBeacon BOFschevron-left](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/beacon/beacon-bofs)
[NextGopher BOFschevron-right](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/gopher/gopher-bofs)

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [Configuration](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/gopher#configuration)
    
*   [Commands](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/extenders/agents/gopher#commands)

# Gopher BOFs | Adaptix Framework

**AX BOF APIs:**

Copy

    void AxAddScreenshot(char* note, char* data, int len);
    void AxDownloadMemory(char* filename, char* data, int len);

**Beacon currently supports the following BOF APIs:**

Copy

    // Data Parser API
    char* BeaconDataExtract (datap * parser, int * size)
    int BeaconDataInt (datap * parser)
    int BeaconDataLength (datap * parser)
    void BeaconDataParse (datap * parser, char * buffer, int size)
    short BeaconDataShort (datap * parser)
    
    // Output API
    void BeaconPrintf (int type, char * fmt, ...)
    void BeaconOutput (int type, char * data, int len)
    
    //  Format API
    void BeaconFormatAlloc (formatp * obj, int maxsz)
    void BeaconFormatAppend (formatp * obj, char * data, int len)
    void BeaconFormatFree (formatp * obj)
    void BeaconFormatInt (formatp * obj, int val)
    void BeaconFormatPrintf (formatp * obj, char * fmt, ...)
    void BeaconFormatReset (formatp * obj)
    char* BeaconFormatToString (formatp * obj, int * size)
    
    // Internal APIs
    BOOL BeaconUseToken (HANDLE token)
    void BeaconRevertToken ()
    BOOL BeaconIsAdmin ()
    BOOL toWideChar (char * src, wchar_t * dst, int max)
    
    BOOL BeaconAddValue (const char * key, void * ptr);
    void* BeaconGetValue (const char * key);
    BOOL BeaconRemoveValue (const char * key);

**Unsupported BOF APIs:**

# Register new extenders | Adaptix Framework

Templates for developing your own Extenders agents and listeners are located in [THISarrow-up-right](https://github.com/Adaptix-Framework/templates-extender)
 repository. Since Extenders uses goplugin technology, the core framework package versions and all extenders must be the same. Go Workspace technology is used to easily manage large numbers of extenders.

All actions are performed in the `AdaptixServer` directory.

1.  Move your extenders in the `AdaptixServer/extenders` directory and add them to the workspace.
    

Copy

    go work use extenders/new_listener_extender
    go work use extenders/new_agent_extender
    go work use extenders/new_service_extender

1.  Sync Go Workspace
    

Copy

    go work sync

1.  Build the extenders and specify the path to the `config.yaml` in the server profile.
    

Copy

    make extenders

* * *

Last updated 2 months ago

---

# Extenders | Adaptix Framework

Guide for developing extenders for AdaptixC2: Listener, Agent, and Service Extender.

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FDUpgTg2r2taOKRyvEXOn%252FScreenshot_20260120_215032.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfbf37ffa-a31b-4797-aec7-6325a9fd8f5d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=23bccc33&sv=2)

Copy

    ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                              ADAPTIX SERVER                                     │
    ├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
    │                                                                                 │
    │  ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
    │  │                         EXTENDER MANAGER                                  │  │
    │  ├───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤  │
    │  │                                                                           │  │
    │  │   LoadPlugins() ───┬──> LoadPluginListener() ──> PluginListener Interface │  │
    │  │                    ├──> LoadPluginAgent()    ──> PluginAgent Interface    │  │
    │  │                    └──> LoadPluginService()  ──> PluginService Interface  │  │
    │  │                                                                           │  │
    │  │   ┌─────────────┐       ┌─────────────┐       ┌─────────────┐             │  │
    │  │   │   config    │       │   plugin    │       │   .axs      │             │  │
    │  │   │   .yaml     │       │   .so       │       │   UI file   │             │  │
    │  │   └─────────────┘       └─────────────┘       └─────────────┘             │  │
    │  │                                │                                          │  │
    │  │                                V                                          │  │
    │  │                    InitPlugin(ts, moduleDir, ...)                         │  │
    │  │                                │                                          │  │
    │  │   ┌────────────────────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────┐  │  │
    │  │   │                                                                    │  │  │
    │  │   │   ┌─────────────────┐  ┌────────────────┐  ┌───────────────────┐   │  │  │
    │  │   │   │Listener Extender│  │ Agent Extender │  │  Service Extender │   │  │  │
    │  │   │   │                 │  │                │  │                   │   │  │  │
    │  │   │   │ PluginListener  │  │  PluginAgent   │  │   PluginService   │   │  │  │
    │  │   │   └─────────────────┘  └────────────────┘  └───────────────────┘   │  │  │
    │  │   └────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │  │
    │  │                                                                           │  │
    │  └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
    │                                                                                 │
    │  ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │
    │  │                         EVENT MANAGER                                     │  │
    │  ├───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤  │
    │  │                                                                           │  │
    │  │   ┌─────────────┐       ┌─────────────┐       ┌─────────────┐             │  │
    │  │   │  Pre Hooks  │──────>│   Action    │──────>│ Post Hooks  │             │  │
    │  │   └─────────────┘       └─────────────┘       └─────────────┘             │  │
    │  │                                                                           │  │
    │  │   TsEventHookRegister(event, phase, priority, handler)                    │  │
    │  │                                                                           │  │
    │  └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │
    │                                                                                 │
    └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

**Listener**

# Internal listener | Adaptix Framework

Internal Listener defines the protocol for pivot connections (SMB pipe, TCP). Does not open ports on the server.

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/extenders/listener-extender/internal-listener#flow-diagram)

Flow Diagram

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252Fl3ekQ6qa6COmRjczk390%252FScreenshot_20260120_205625.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7429f64f-04cb-4d77-8158-aa98b8449967&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b8ae622f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/extenders/listener-extender/internal-listener#differences-from-external-listener)

Differences from External Listener

Aspect

External Listener

Internal Listener

Opens ports

Yes (HTTP, DNS)

No

Connection

Agent → Server directly

Via parent agent

`InternalHandler()`

Returns empty string

Creates child agent

Examples

HTTP, HTTPS, DNS

SMB, TCP (pivot)

* * *

[NextAgent pluginchevron-right](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/extenders/agent-plugin)

    ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                          INTERNAL LISTENER FLOW                                  │
    ├──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
    │                                                                                  │

    │                                                                                  │
    │  GUI ──> POST /listener/create                                                   │
    │                   │                                                              │
    │                   V                                                              │
    │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
    │  │ TEAMSERVER                                                                  │ │
    │  │         │                                                                   │ │
    │  │         V                                                                   │ │
    │  │  TsListenerCreate(listenerType, name, config)                               │ │
    │  │         │                                                                   │ │
    │  │         V                                                                   │ │
    │  │  ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │ │
    │  │  │ EXTENDER                                                              │  │ │
    │  │  │         │                                                             │  │ │
    │  │  │         V                                                             │  │ │
    │  │  │  PluginListener.Create(name, config, customData)                      │  │ │
    │  │  │         │                                                             │  │ │
    │  │  │         └──> Save configuration (pipename, encrypt_key, etc.)         │  │ │
    │  │  │              Does NOT open ports/pipes on the server!                 │  │ │
    │  │  │                                                                       │  │ │
    │  │  └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘  │ │
    │  │                                                                             │ │
    │  └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘ │
    │                                                                                  │
    │  ╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗  │
    │  ║                          PIVOT AGENT CONNECTION                            ║  │
    │  ╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝  │
    │                                                                                  │
    │  Child Agent ──> COMMAND_LINK via Parent Agent                                   │
    │                   │                                                              │
    │                   V                                                              │
    │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐ │
    │  │ EXTENDER (Agent Plugin)                                                     │ │
    │  │         │                                                                   │ │
    │  │         V                                                                   │ │
    │  │  ExtenderAgent.ProcessData() ──> ProcessTasksResult()                       │ │
    │  │         │                                                                   │ │
    │  │         V                                                                   │ │
    │  │  case COMMAND_LINK:                                                         │ │
    │  │         │                                                                   │ │
    │  │         ├──> watermark := packer.ParseInt32()                               │ │
    │  │         ├──> data := packer.ParseBytes()                                    │ │
    │  │         │                                                                   │ │
    │  │         V                                                                   │ │
    │  │  ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │ │
    │  │  │ TEAMSERVER                                                            │  │ │
    │  │  │         │                                                             │  │ │
    │  │  │         V                                                             │  │ │
    │  │  │  TsListenerInteralHandler(watermark, data)                            │  │ │
    │  │  │         │                                                             │  │ │
    │  │  │         V                                                             │  │ │
    │  │  │  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐  │  │ │
