[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#tabs)

Tabs


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `tabs` element provides a stack of tabbed widgets.

`element form.create_tabs()` - Constructs a `tabs` element.

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#methods-17)

Methods:

1

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#addtab)

addTab

* * *

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#stack)

Stack


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `stack` element provides a stack of widgets where only one widget is visible at a time.

`element create_stack()` - Constructs a `stack`.

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#methods-18)

Methods:

1

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#addpage-1)

addPage

Appends the given `page` to the `stask` and returns the index position.

2

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#insertpage)

insertPage

Inserts the given `page` at the given `index` in the `stack`.

3

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#removepage)

removePage

Removes element from the `stack` by `index`.

4

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setcurrentindex-1)

setCurrentIndex

This method set the `index` position of the widget that is visible;

5

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#currentindex-1)

currentIndex

This method return the `index` position of the widget that is visible;

6

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#count-1)

count

This method return the number of elements contained by this `stack`.

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#signals-9)

Signals:

1

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#currentchanged)

currentChanged

This signal is emitted whenever the current element changes.

chevron-rightExample[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#example-22)

![](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2104178602-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FS8p8XLFtLmf0NkofQvoa%252Fuploads%252FkpSwggVHQkbNiTZ9KIxL%252FScreenshot_20250726_012107.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd265f63e-435c-488d-bb6e-88f8fbfb6f97&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=40f39975&sv=2)

* * *

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#dialog)

Dialog


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `dialog` element is implement of dialog windows.

`dialog create_dialog(string title)` - Constructs a `dialog` with `title`.

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#methods-19)

Methods:

1

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setbuttonstext)

setButtonsText

This method sets the text `ok_text` for button OK and the text `cancel_text` for button CANCEL.

2

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setsize)

setSize

This method sets the size for the window.

3

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#setlayout-1)

setLayout

Sets the layout manager for this window.

4

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#close)

close

Close window.

5

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/axscript/axform-type#exec)

exec

Shows the dialog as a modal dialog, blocking until the user closes it. If the window is closed by pressing the OK button, the method will return true.

    form.create_container()

Copy

    void container::put(string id, element elem);

Copy

    element container::get(string id);

Copy

    bool container::contains(string id)

Copy

    void container::remove(string id)

Copy

    string container::toJson();

Copy

    void container::fromJson(string jsonString);

Copy

    let tl1 = form.create_textline();
    let tl2 = form.create_textline();
    let tm3 = form.create_textmulti();
    let btn = form.create_button("Get data");
    
    let container = form.create_container()
    container.put("line1", tl1)
    container.put("lin2", tl2)
    
    form.connect(btn, "clicked", function(){
        tm3.setText(container.toJson());
    });
    
    let layout = form.create_vlayout();
    layout.addWidget(tl1);
    layout.addWidget(tl2);
    layout.addWidget(tm3);
    layout.addWidget(btn);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

    let b1 = form.create_button("One");
    let b2 = form.create_button("Two");
    let b3 = form.create_button("Three");
    let b4 = form.create_button("Four");
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();

    layout.addWidget(b2, 0, 2, 2, 1);
    layout.addWidget(b3, 1, 0, 1, 1);
    layout.addWidget(b4, 1, 1, 1, 1);

    dialog.exec()

    let c1 = form.create_check("Checkbox");
    
    let tl2 = form.create_textline();
    tl2.setReadOnly(true);
    
    form.connect(c1, "stateChanged", function(){
        if(c1.isChecked())
            tl2.setText("Checked");
        else
            tl2.setText("UnChecked");
    });
    
    let layout = form.create_vlayout();
    layout.addWidget(c1);
    layout.addWidget(tl2);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

    let listw = form.create_list();
    listw.addItems(["Item 1", "Item 2", "Item 3"]);
    listw.addItem("New");
    
    let text_line   = form.create_textline(listw.count())
    let text_button = form.create_button("go");
    
    form.connect(text_button, "clicked", function (){
        text_line.setText(listw.items());
    })
    
    form.connect(listw, "itemClicked", function (text){
        text_line.setText(text);
    })
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(listw,     0, 0, 1, 2);
    layout.addWidget(text_line, 1, 0, 1, 1);
    layout.addWidget(text_button, 1, 1, 1, 1);

    dialog.setSize(460, 240);

Copy

    let table = form.create_table(["Name", "Age", "Id"])
    table.addItem(["Alex", "23", "a1a2"]);
    table.addItem(["Bella", "37", "b1c8"]);
    table.setColumnAlign(1, "center");
    
    let text_line   = form.create_textline(table.columnCount())
    let text_button = form.create_button("go");
    
    form.connect(text_button, "clicked", function (){
        text_line.setText(table.selectedRows());
    })
    
    form.connect(table, "cellChanged", function (row, column){
        text_line.setText(table.text(row, column));
    })
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(table,     0, 0, 1, 2);
    layout.addWidget(text_line, 1, 0, 1, 1);
    layout.addWidget(text_button, 1, 1, 1, 1);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setSize(460, 240);
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

    let text_multi1 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 1");
    let combo_w = form.create_combo();
    combo_w.setItems(["Panel 1", "Panel 2"]);
    
    let layout1 = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout1.addWidget(text_multi1, 0, 0, 1, 1);
    layout1.addWidget(combo_w,     1, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let panel = form.create_panel();
    panel.setLayout(layout1);
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(panel, 0, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setSize(460, 240);
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

Copy

    bool groupbox::isChecked();

Copy

    void groupbox::setChecked(bool checked);

Copy

    bool groupbox::isCheckable();

Copy

    void groupbox::setCheckable(bool checkable);

Copy

    void groupbox::setTitle(string title);

Copy

    void groupbox::setPanel(element panel);

Copy

    clicked(bool checked = false);

Copy

    let text_multi1 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 1");
    let combo_w = form.create_combo();
    combo_w.setItems(["Panel 1", "Panel 2"]);
    
    let layout1 = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout1.addWidget(text_multi1, 0, 0, 1, 1);
    layout1.addWidget(combo_w,     1, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let panel = form.create_panel();
    panel.setLayout(layout1);
    
    let group_box = form.create_groupbox("Box", true);
    group_box.setPanel(panel);
    
    form.connect(group_box, "clicked", function (checked){
        panel.setEnabled(checked);
    })
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(group_box, 0, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setSize(460, 240);
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

Copy

    void scrollarea::setWidgetResizable(bool resizable);

Copy

    void scrollarea::setPanel(element panel);

Copy

    let text_multi1 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 1");
    let text_multi2 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 2");
    let combo_w = form.create_combo();
    combo_w.setItems(["Panel 1", "Panel 2"]);
    
    
    let layout1 = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout1.addWidget(text_multi1, 0, 0, 1, 1);
    layout1.addWidget(text_multi2,     1, 0, 1, 1);
    layout1.addWidget(combo_w,     2, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let panel = form.create_panel();
    panel.setLayout(layout1);
    
    
    const scroll = form.create_scrollarea();
    scroll.setPanel(panel);
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(scroll, 0, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setSize(460, 240);
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

Copy

    void splitter::setSizes(int[] sizes);

Copy

    void splitter::addPage(element elem);

Copy

    splitterMoved(int pos, int index)

Copy

    let text_multi1 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 1");
    let text_multi2 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 2");
    
    let splitter = form.create_hsplitter();
    splitter.addPage(text_multi1);
    splitter.addPage(text_multi2);
    splitter.setSizes([100, 200]);
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(splitter, 0, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setSize(460, 240);
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

Copy

    void tabs::addTab(element elem, string title)

Copy

    let text_multi1 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 1");
    let text_multi2 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 2");
    
    let tabs = form.create_tabs();
    tabs.addTab(text_multi1, "tab 1");
    tabs.addTab(text_multi2, "tab 2");
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(tabs, 0, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setSize(460, 240);
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

Copy

    int stack::addPage(element page);

Copy

    int stack::insertPage(int index, element page);

Copy

    void stack::removePage(int index);

Copy

    void stack::setCurrentIndex(int index);

Copy

    int stack::currentIndex();

Copy

    int stack::count();

Copy

    currentChanged(int index);

Copy

    let text_multi1 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 1");
    let text_multi2 = form.create_textmulti("Panel 2");
    
    let stack_w = form.create_stack();
    stack_w.addPage(text_multi1);
    stack_w.addPage(text_multi2);
    
    let combo_w = form.create_combo();
    combo_w.setItems(["Panel 1", "Panel 2"]);
    
    form.connect(combo_w, "currentIndexChanged", function (index){
        stack_w.setCurrentIndex(index);
    })
    
    let layout = form.create_gridlayout();
    layout.addWidget(stack_w,   0, 0, 1, 1);
    layout.addWidget(combo_w, 1, 0, 1, 1);
    
    let dialog = form.create_dialog("");
    dialog.setSize(460, 240);
    dialog.setLayout(layout);
    dialog.exec()

# TS API | Adaptix Framework

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#agent-functions)

Agent Functions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentisexists)

TsAgentIsExists

Checks if an agent exists by ID.

Copy

    TsAgentIsExists(agentId string) bool

Parameter

Type

Description

`agentId`

`string`

Unique agent identifier

**Returns:** `bool` — `true` if agent exists

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentcreate)

TsAgentCreate

Creates a new agent on first connection.

Copy

    TsAgentCreate(agentCrc string, agentId string, beat []byte, listenerName string, ExternalIP string, Async bool) (adaptix.AgentData, error)

Parameter

Type

Description

`agentCrc`

`string`

CRC/watermark of agent type

`agentId`

`string`

Unique agent ID

`beat`

`[]byte`

Initial data from agent (heartbeat)

`listenerName`

`string`

Listener name

`ExternalIP`

`string`

Agent's external IP

`Async`

`bool`

Async mode

**Returns:** `adaptix.AgentData`, `error`

**Events:**

*   `agent.new` (Pre/Post hooks)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentprocessdata)

TsAgentProcessData

Processes data received from the agent.

Parameter

Type

Description

`agentId`

`string`

Agent ID

`bodyData`

`[]byte`

Data from agent

**Note:** If the agent has `Mark="Inactive"`, it is automatically activated and the `agent.activate` event is called.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentupdatedata)

TsAgentUpdateData

Updates agent data (sleep, jitter, killdate, workingtime).

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentupdatedatapartial)

TsAgentUpdateDataPartial

Partial update of agent data.

**Supported fields:**

*   `InternalIP`, `ExternalIP`, `GmtOffset`, `ACP`, `OemCP`
    
*   `Pid`, `Tid`, `Arch`, `Elevated`, `Process`
    
*   `Os`, `OsDesc`, `Domain`, `Computer`, `Username`
    
*   `Impersonated`, `Tags`, `Mark`, `Color`
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentterminate)

TsAgentTerminate

Terminates the agent.

**Actions on call:**

1.  Cancels all active downloads
    
2.  Stops all tunnels
    
3.  Closes terminals
    
4.  Clears task queues
    
5.  Removes pivot connections
    

**Events:**

*   `agent.terminate` (Pre/Post hooks)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentsettick)

TsAgentSetTick

Updates the agent's last response time and current listener.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentconsoleoutput)

TsAgentConsoleOutput

Outputs a message to the agent console.

Parameter

Type

Description

`agentId`

`string`

Agent ID

`messageType`

`int`

Message type (5=INFO, 6=ERROR, 7=SUCCESS)

`message`

`string`

Message title

`clearText`

`string`

Message text

`store`

`bool`

Store in DB

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentbuildexecute)

TsAgentBuildExecute

Executes an external command during agent build with output redirected to the WebSocket build channel.

Parameter

Type

Description

`builderId`

`string`

Builder ID (empty string for synchronous execution)

`workingDir`

`string`

Working directory for the command

`program`

`string`

Executable

`args`

`...string`

Command-line arguments

**Note:** If `builderId` is empty, the command executes synchronously without WebSocket output. Otherwise, stdout/stderr are redirected to the build channel.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentbuildlog)

TsAgentBuildLog

Sends a log message to the agent's WebSocket build channel.

Parameter

Type

Description

`builderId`

`string`

Builder ID

`status`

`int`

Status: BUILD\_LOG\_NONE=0, INFO=1, ERROR=2, SUCCESS=3

`message`

`string`

Message text

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentgethosted-functions)

TsAgentGetHosted\* Functions

Gets tasks for sending to the agent. All functions pack tasks considering size limitations.

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentgethostedall)

**TsAgentGetHostedAll**

Gets all available tasks: regular tasks, tunnel tasks, tunnel data, and pivot tasks.

Parameter

Type

Description

`agentId`

`string`

Agent ID

`maxDataSize`

`int`

Maximum data size (bytes)

**Returns:** Packed task data for sending to the agent.

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentgethostedtasks)

**TsAgentGetHostedTasks**

Gets only regular tasks and tunnel tasks (without pivot).

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsagentgethostedtaskscount)

**TsAgentGetHostedTasksCount**

Gets the specified number of tasks.

Parameter

Type

Description

`agentId`

`string`

Agent ID

`count`

`int`

Maximum number of tasks

`maxDataSize`

`int`

Maximum data size (bytes)

* * *

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#task-functions)

Task Functions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tstaskrunningexists)

TsTaskRunningExists

Checks if a task is running.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tstaskcreate)

TsTaskCreate

Creates a new task.

**Events:**

*   `task.create` (Pre/Post hooks)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tstaskupdate)

TsTaskUpdate

Updates the task with execution results.

**Events:**

*   `task.complete` (Post hook) — when task is completed
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tstaskcancel)

TsTaskCancel

Cancels a task that is in the queue (not yet sent to the agent).

Parameter

Type

Description

`agentId`

`string`

Agent ID

`taskId`

`string`

Task ID

**Note:** Cancels only tasks in the queue. Already running tasks cannot be cancelled.

* * *

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#client-gui-functions)

Client GUI Functions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Functions for synchronizing data with GUI clients (File Browser, Process Manager). These functions send results only to the client that initiated the request.

Download/Upload Functions

*   `download.start` (Pre/Post hooks)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsdownloadupdate)

TsDownloadUpdate

Updates download state.

State

Value

Description

1

RUNNING

Download in progress

2

STOPPED

Paused

3

FINISHED

Completed

4

CANCELED

Cancelled

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsdownloadclose)

TsDownloadClose

Finishes a download.

**Events:**

*   `download.finish` (Pre/Post hooks)
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsdownloadsave)

TsDownloadSave

Saves a file directly (from memory).

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsdownloadgetfilepath)

TsDownloadGetFilepath

Returns the local path to the downloaded file.

Parameter

Type

Description

`fileId`

`string`

File ID

**Returns:** Full path to the file on the server.

**Note:** Works only for completed downloads (state=FINISHED).

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsdownloaddelete)

TsDownloadDelete

Deletes downloaded files.

Parameter

Type

Description

`fileId`

`[]string`

List of file IDs

**Actions:**

1.  Deletes files from disk
    
2.  Removes records from DB
    
3.  Synchronizes with clients
    

**Events:**

*   `download.remove` (Pre/Post hooks)

Password (if UseAuth)

#### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tstunnelcreatelportfwd)

TsTunnelCreateLportfwd

Type

Description

`AgentId`

`string`

Agent ID

`Info`

`string`

Tunnel description

`Lhost`

`string`

Local address

`Lport`

`int`

Local port

`Thost`

`string`

Target address (on agent)

`Tport`

`int`

Target port

`string`

Agent ID

`string`

`int`

AxScript Server Functions


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Server-side AxScript engine functions. Allow loading and executing scripts on the server side, defining commands and hooks without client participation.

Description

`string`

Script name

Script content

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsaxscriptlist)

TsAxScriptList

Returns a JSON list of loaded scripts.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsaxscriptcommands)

TsAxScriptCommands

Returns a JSON list of registered server-side commands.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsaxscriptresolvehooks)

TsAxScriptResolveHooks

Resolves server-side hooks for an agent command. Used when processing commands where the client did not provide a hook/handler.

Parameter

Type

Description

`agentName`

`string`

Agent type name

`agentId`

`string`

Agent ID

`listenerRegName`

`string`

Registered listener name

`os`

`int`

Agent OS type

`cmdline`

`string`

Command line

`args`

`map[string]interface{}`

Command arguments

**Returns:** `hookId`, `handlerId`, `preHookHandled` (true if Pre hook fully handled the command), `error`

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsaxscriptparseandexecute)

TsAxScriptParseAndExecute

Parses and executes a raw command via the server-side AxScript engine.

Parameter

Type

Description

`agentId`

`string`

Agent ID

`username`

`string`

Operator name

`cmdline`

`string`

Command line

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#axgetagentcontext)

AxGetAgentContext

Returns agent context for the server-side AxScript.

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#endpoint-functions)

Endpoint Functions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Functions for registering HTTP endpoints.

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsendpointregister)

TsEndpointRegister

Registers a protected endpoint (uses the teamserver's shared JWT authentication).

Parameter

Type

Description

`method`

`string`

HTTP method (GET, POST...)

`path`

`string`

Endpoint path

`handler`

`func(username string, body []byte) (int, []byte)`

Handler

**Handler parameters:**

*   `username` — authenticated username
    
*   `body` — request body
    

**Handler returns:**

*   `int` — HTTP status code
    
*   `[]byte` — response body
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsendpointunregister)

TsEndpointUnregister

Unregisters an endpoint.

HTTP method (GET, POST...)

Utility Functions


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsconvertcptoutf8)

TsConvertCpToUTF8

Converts a string from a code page to UTF-8.

**Supported code pages:**

*   866 (Russian DOS)
    
*   1251 (Cyrillic Windows)
    
*   1252 (Western European Windows)
    
*   936 (Chinese GBK)
    
*   65001 (UTF-8)
    
*   and many others...
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tsconvertutf8tocp)

TsConvertUTF8toCp

Converts UTF-8 to the agent's code page.

* * *

[hashtag](https://adaptix-framework.gitbook.io/adaptix-framework/development/teamserver-interface/ts-api#tswin32error)

TsWin32Error

Returns a description of a Windows error code.

    type AgentData struct {
        Crc          string   // CRC/watermark of the agent type
        Id           string   // Unique agent ID
        Name         string   // Agent type name
        SessionKey   []byte   // Session key for encryption
        Listener     string   // Listener name
        Async        bool     // Asynchronous mode
        ExternalIP   string   // External IP address
        InternalIP   string   // Internal IP address
        GmtOffset    int      // Time zone offset
        Sleep        uint     // Sleep interval (seconds)
        Jitter       uint     // Jitter (percentage)
        Pid          string   // Process ID
        Tid          string   // Thread ID
        Arch         string   // Architecture (x86, x64)
        Elevated     bool     // Elevated privileges
        Process      string   // Process name
        Os           int      // OS type (0=Windows, 1=Linux, 2=macOS)
        OsDesc       string   // OS description
        Domain       string   // Domain
        Computer     string   // Computer name
        Username     string   // Username
        Impersonated string   // Impersonated user
        OemCP        int      // OEM code page
        ACP          int      // ANSI code page
        CreateTime   int64    // Creation time (Unix timestamp)
        LastTick     int      // Last tick
        KillDate     int      // Kill date
        WorkingTime  int      // Working time
        Tags         string   // Tags
        Mark         string   // Mark (Inactive, Terminated, etc.)
        Color        string   // Color in GUI
        TargetId     string   // ID of the associated target
    }

Copy

    type TaskData struct {
        Type        int      // Type: TASK_TYPE_TASK=1, TASK_TYPE_BROWSER=2, TASK_TYPE_JOB=3, TASK_TYPE_TUNNEL=4
        TaskId      string   // Unique task ID
        AgentId     string   // Agent ID
        Client      string   // Client (operator) name
        HookId      string   // Hook ID for callback
        HandlerId   string   // Handler ID for callback
        User        string   // User on the target machine
        Computer    string   // Computer name
        StartDate   int64    // Start time
        FinishDate  int64    // Finish time
        Data        []byte   // Task binary data
        CommandLine string   // Command line
        MessageType int      // Message type: INFO=5, ERROR=6, SUCCESS=7
        Message     string   // Message title
        ClearText   string   // Message text
        Completed   bool     // Completion flag
        Sync        bool     // Synchronize with GUI
    }

Copy

    type ListenerData struct {
        Name       string   // Unique listener name
        RegName    string   // Registered type
        Protocol   string   // Protocol
        Type       string   // Listener type
        BindHost   string   // Bind address
        BindPort   string   // Bind port
        AgentAddr  string   // Address for the agent
        CreateTime int64    // Creation date
        Status     string   // Status (running, stopped, paused)
        Data       string   // Additional data (JSON)
        Watermark  string   // Watermark
    }

Copy

    type DownloadData struct {
        FileId     string   // Unique file ID
        AgentId    string   // Agent ID
        AgentName  string   // Agent type name
        User       string   // User
        Computer   string   // Computer
        RemotePath string   // Path on the target machine
        LocalPath  string   // Local path on the server
        TotalSize  int      // Total file size
        RecvSize   int      // Received size
        Date       int64    // Start date
        State      int      // State: RUNNING=1, STOPPED=2, FINISHED=3, CANCELED=4
    }

Copy

    type TunnelData struct {
        TunnelId  string   // Unique tunnel ID
        AgentId   string   // Agent ID
        Computer  string   // Computer
        Username  string   // User
        Process   string   // Process
        Type      string   // Type (socks4, socks5, lportfwd, rportfwd)
        Info      string   // Additional information
        Interface string   // Bind interface
        Port      string   // Port
        Client    string   // Client that created the tunnel
        Fhost     string   // Forward host
        Fport     string   // Forward port
        AuthUser  string   // Authentication user
        AuthPass  string   // Authentication password
    }

Copy

    type PivotData struct {
        PivotId       string   // Unique pivot ID
        PivotName     string   // Pivot name
        ParentAgentId string   // Parent agent ID
        ChildAgentId  string   // Child agent ID
    }

Copy

    type CredsData struct {
        CredId   string   // Unique ID
        Username string   // Username
        Password string   // Password or hash
        Realm    string   // Domain/realm
        Type     string   // Type (NTLM, Plaintext, Kerberos)
        Tag      string   // Tag
        Date     int64    // Date added
        Storage  string   // Source (LSASS, SAM, DCSync)
        AgentId  string   // Agent ID (source)
        Host     string   // Host (source)
    }

Copy

    type TargetData struct {
        TargetId string     // Unique target ID
        Computer string     // Computer name
        Domain   string     // Domain
        Address  string     // IP address
        Os       int        // OS type
        OsDesk   string     // OS description
        Tag      string     // Tag
        Info     string     // Additional information
        Date     int64      // Date added
        Alive    bool       // Active
        Agents   []string   // List of agent IDs
    }

Copy

    // Task types
    const (
        TASK_TYPE_TASK    = 1   // Regular task
        TASK_TYPE_BROWSER = 2   // File/Process Browser
        TASK_TYPE_JOB     = 3   // Background job
        TASK_TYPE_TUNNEL  = 4   // Tunnel
    )
    
    // Console message types
    const (
        CONSOLE_OUT_LOCAL         = 1
        CONSOLE_OUT_LOCAL_INFO    = 2
        CONSOLE_OUT_LOCAL_ERROR   = 3
        CONSOLE_OUT_LOCAL_SUCCESS = 4
        CONSOLE_OUT_INFO          = 5   // INFO
        CONSOLE_OUT_ERROR         = 6   // ERROR
        CONSOLE_OUT_SUCCESS       = 7   // SUCCESS
        CONSOLE_OUT               = 10
    )
    
    // Download states
    const (
        DOWNLOAD_STATE_RUNNING  = 1
        DOWNLOAD_STATE_STOPPED  = 2
        DOWNLOAD_STATE_FINISHED = 3
        DOWNLOAD_STATE_CANCELED = 4
    )
